## Australia - Family Visa

VISA TYPE: Australian Family Visas - Child, Remaining Relative, NZ Citizen Family
COUNTRY: Australia
SOURCE: https://immi.homeaffairs.gov.au/visas/getting-a-visa/visa-listing/
LAST UPDATED: 2024

=== VISA SUBCLASSES OVERVIEW ===

---CHUNK: Australia_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_1---
## Australia - Family Visa

UPDATED: 2024

=== VISA SUBCLASSES OVERVIEW ===

SUBCLASS 445 - DEPENDENT CHILD VISA (TEMPORARY):
• Purpose: Allows child to stay temporarily while parent's permanent Partner visa (100/801) is processed
• Stay: Temporary, until decision on parent's permanent visa
• Cost: From AUD 3,235
• Apply: Paper application only
• Requirement: Child's parent must hold temporary Partner visa (309/820) or dependent child visa

---CHUNK: Australia_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_2---
## Australia - Family Visa

y Partner visa (309/820) or dependent child visa

SUBCLASS 101 - CHILD VISA (OFFSHORE):
• Purpose: Child outside Australia moves to Australia to live with parent(s)
• Stay: Permanent residence
• Cost: From AUD 3,235
• Apply: Paper application only; must be OUTSIDE Australia when applying and when decided
• Sponsor: Eligible parent who is Australian citizen/PR/eligible NZ citizen

who is Australian citizen/PR/eligible NZ citizen

SUBCLASS 802 - CHILD VISA (ONSHORE):
• Purpose: Child already in Australia stays permanently with parent(s)
• Stay: Permanent residence
• Cost: From AUD 3,235
• Apply: Paper application only; must be INSIDE Australia when applying and when decided
• Sponsor: Eligible parent who is Australian citizen/PR/eligible NZ citizen

who is Australian citizen/PR/eligible NZ citizen

SUBCLASS 102 - ADOPTION VISA:
• Purpose: Child adopted (or in process of adoption) outside Australia moves to Australia with adoptive parent
• Stay: Permanent residence
• Cost: From AUD 3,235
• Apply: Paper application only; child must be OUTSIDE Australia
• Requirement: Adoption must comply with Hague Convention or bilateral arrangement

SUBCLASS 115 - REMAINING RELATIVE VISA (OFFSHORE):
• Purpose: Person moves to Australia to be with their only close family members
• Stay: Permanent residence
• Cost: From AUD 5,280
• Apply: Paper application; must be OUTSIDE Australia when applying and when decided
• Queue wait: Up to 50 years (Other Family Visa Queue)

SUBCLASS 461 - NEW ZEALAND CITIZEN FAMILY RELATIONSHIP VISA:
• Purpose: Non-NZ citizen who is member of family unit of NZ citizen lives/works in Australia
• Stay: Temporary, up to 5 years (renewable)
• Cost: From AUD 445
• Apply: Online or paper; can apply inside OR outside Australia
• Rights: Live, work, study in Australia; travel freely while valid

=== ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA ===

---CHUNK: Australia_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_8---
## Australia - Family Visa

freely while valid

=== ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA ===

CHILD VISAS (101, 802, 445):
□ Child must be under 18, OR 18-25 and financially dependent, OR 18+ with disability preventing self-support
□ Child must be single (not married/in de facto relationship)
□ Child must be sponsored by eligible parent (Australian citizen/PR/eligible NZ citizen)
□ Parent must have legal right to determine child's residence (custody/guardianship)
□ For subclass 802/445: Child must hold eligible substantive visa if applying onshore
□ Health and character requirements apply

---CHUNK: Australia_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_9---
## Australia - Family Visa

nshore
□ Health and character requirements apply

ADOPTION VISA (102):
□ Child must be under 18 at time of application
□ Adoption must be full/legal adoption (not de facto or customary)
□ Adoption must comply with Hague Convention or bilateral arrangement with Australia
□ Adoptive parent must be Australian citizen/PR/eligible NZ citizen
□ At least one adoptive parent must be settled in Australia
□ Health and character requirements apply

---CHUNK: Australia_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_10---
## Australia - Family Visa

tralia
□ Health and character requirements apply

REMAINING RELATIVE VISAS (115, 835):
□ Applicant must be 18+ years old
□ Applicant must have NO near relatives (spouse, children, parents, siblings) living outside Australia
□ "Near relatives" in Australia must be Australian citizen/PR/eligible NZ citizen
□ Must be sponsored by eligible relative in Australia
□ Must meet Balance of Family Test implications (all/near relatives in Australia)
□ Health and character requirements apply
□ Queue wait: Up to 50 years (non-contributory family queue)

---CHUNK: Australia_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_11---
## Australia - Family Visa

: Up to 50 years (non-contributory family queue)

NEW ZEALAND CITIZEN FAMILY RELATIONSHIP (461):
□ Applicant must NOT be a New Zealand citizen
□ Applicant must be member of family unit of NZ citizen who holds Special Category Visa (subclass 444)
• Family unit includes: spouse/de facto partner, dependent child, or dependent relative
□ NZ citizen family member must be living in Australia or intending to live in Australia
□ Applicant must meet health and character requirements
□ No sponsorship required, but must demonstrate family relationship

---CHUNK: Australia_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_12---
## Australia - Family Visa

quired, but must demonstrate family relationship

=== SPONSORSHIP REQUIREMENTS ===
SPONSOR MUST:
□ Be Australian citizen, permanent resident, or eligible New Zealand citizen
□ Be 18+ years old
□ Provide Assurance of Support (AoS) for most family visas (financial bond ~AUD 10,000-14,000)
□ Agree to provide financial/emotional support for first 2 years after grant
□ Not be barred from sponsoring (previous sponsorship failures, criminal history)

---CHUNK: Australia_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_13---
## Australia - Family Visa

previous sponsorship failures, criminal history)

ASSURANCE OF SUPPORT (AoS):
• Required for: Child visas (101/802), Remaining Relative visas (115/835)
• Not required for: Subclass 461 (NZ Citizen Family)
• Amount: ~AUD 10,400 for primary applicant, ~AUD 4,500 for each additional adult
• Held by government for 2 years; refunded if no social security claims made

=== HEALTH & CHARACTER REQUIREMENTS ===
HEALTH:
• Medical examination required for all permanent family visa applicants
• Must be done by Bupa Medical Visa Services panel physician
• Includes chest x-ray (age 11+), HIV test (age 15+), full medical (age 75+)
• Results valid for 12 months

medical (age 75+)
• Results valid for 12 months

CHARACTER:
• Police certificate required from every country lived in 12+ months during past 10 years (since age 16)
• Must declare ALL criminal history, including spent convictions and minor offences
• False/misleading information can result in refusal + 3-year ban

---CHUNK: Australia_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_16---
## Australia - Family Visa

g information can result in refusal + 3-year ban

=== APPLICATION PROCESS ===
PAPER APPLICATIONS (MOST FAMILY VISAS):
1. Download correct form from ImmiAccount:
   - Form 47CH: Child visa (101/802)
   - Form 47OA: Adoption visa (102)
   - Form 47SH: Remaining Relative visa (115/835)
2. Complete form + gather supporting documents
3. Mail application to specified address with payment
4. Await acknowledgment + case officer assignment
5. Respond to any requests for additional information
6. Wait for decision (processing times vary significantly by queue)

---CHUNK: Australia_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_17---
## Australia - Family Visa

n (processing times vary significantly by queue)

ONLINE APPLICATION (SUBCLASS 461 ONLY):
1. Create ImmiAccount: https://online.immi.gov.au
2. Complete NZ Citizen Family Relationship visa application
3. Upload supporting documents (relationship proof, NZ citizen's visa status)
4. Pay application charge (AUD 445) by credit card
5. Await decision (typically faster than paper applications)

• NZ Citizen Family Relationship (461): AUD 445
• Assurance of Support bond (if required): ~AUD 10,400 primary + AUD 4,500 per additional adult

• Child visas (101/802): Check visa processing time guide tool; typically 12-24 months
• Adoption visa (102): Varies by country of adoption; typically 12-36 months
• Remaining Relative visas (115/835): Up to 50 years (Other Family Visa Queue)

Family Relationship (461): Typically 3-6 months

=== VISA CONDITIONS (IF GRANTED) ===
CHILD VISAS:
• Full work and study rights upon grant
• Access to Medicare (if eligible)
• Pathway to citizenship after 4 years permanent residence

REMAINING RELATIVE VISAS:
• Full work and study rights
• Access to Medicare and social security (after waiting periods)
• Pathway to citizenship after 4 years permanent residence

## Australia - Family Visa

to citizenship after 4 years permanent residence

SUBCLASS 461 (NZ CITIZEN FAMILY):
• Full work and study rights in Australia
• Travel freely while visa valid
• Must maintain family relationship with NZ citizen holder of subclass 444
• Does NOT lead directly to permanent residence (separate application required)

---CHUNK: Australia_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_22---
## Australia - Family Visa

manent residence (separate application required)

=== PATHWAY TO CITIZENSHIP ===
• After holding permanent family visa for 4 years (including 12 months as PR), may apply for Australian citizenship by conferral
• Must meet residence requirements, character test, and citizenship test
• Children under 16 may be included in parent's citizenship application

---CHUNK: Australia_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_23---
## Australia - Family Visa

be included in parent's citizenship application

=== RESTRICTIONS & RISKS ===
✗ Remaining Relative visas have extreme queue waits (up to 50 years); consider alternative visas if urgent
✗ Child must remain dependent (financially/emotionally) for eligibility; independence may affect status
✗ Adoption must be legally recognized by Australia; informal/customary adoptions not accepted
✗ Subclass 461 is temporary; must reapply every 5 years or transition to another visa for permanence
✗ All family visas require genuine relationship; sham relationships result in refusal + 3-year ban
✗ Overstaying or breaching visa conditions affects future Australian immigration applications

## Australia - Tourist Visa

VISA TYPE: Visitor Visa Subclass 600 - Tourist Stream
COUNTRY: Australia
SOURCE: https://immi.homeaffairs.gov.au/visas/getting-a-visa/visa-listing/visitor-600/tourist
LAST UPDATED: 2024

---CHUNK: Australia_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_1---
## Australia - Tourist Visa

a-listing/visitor-600/tourist
LAST UPDATED: 2024

=== OVERVIEW ===
• Visit Australia for tourism, cruise, or to visit family/friends
• Apply from OUTSIDE Australia (both when applying and when decision is made)
• Stay: Up to 12 months (duration granted at discretion of case officer)
• Cost: From AUD 200 (Visa Application Charge)
• Processing times: Check official tool; varies by country and season

---CHUNK: Australia_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_2---
## Australia - Tourist Visa

heck official tool; varies by country and season

=== ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA ===
APPLICANT MUST:
□ Intend to come to Australia for a genuine temporary visit only
□ Have sufficient funds to cover stay + return travel
□ Not intend to work in Australia (volunteer work may be permitted in limited cases)
□ Be outside Australia when applying AND when visa decision is made
□ Meet health and character requirements
□ Satisfy Genuine Temporary Entrant (GTE) requirement

---CHUNK: Australia_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_3---
## Australia - Tourist Visa

isfy Genuine Temporary Entrant (GTE) requirement

=== GENUINE TEMPORARY ENTRANT (GTE) ASSESSMENT ===
CASE OFFICER WILL CONSIDER:
• Personal circumstances in home country: employment, family ties, community involvement, assets
• Potential incentives to remain in Australia: economic opportunities, family/friends in Australia
• Immigration history: previous compliance with Australian or other countries' visa conditions
• Purpose and plausibility of visit: itinerary, bookings, invitation letters
• Situation in home country vs. Australia: political stability, economic conditions

---CHUNK: Australia_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_4---
## Australia - Tourist Visa

tralia: political stability, economic conditions

=== FINANCIAL REQUIREMENTS ===
PROOF OF FUNDS (ACCEPTABLE DOCUMENTS):
• Bank statements (last 3-6 months) showing consistent balance
• Pay slips or employment letter confirming salary/income
• Sponsorship letter + sponsor's financial documents (if being supported)
• Proof of assets: property deeds, investment statements, business registration
• Pre-paid travel/accommodation bookings (supporting evidence only)

---CHUNK: Australia_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_5---
## Australia - Tourist Visa

ccommodation bookings (supporting evidence only)

GUIDELINE AMOUNTS (NOT OFFICIAL MINIMUM):
• AUD 1,000-1,500 per month of stay for basic living costs
• Plus return airfare or proof of funds to purchase one
• Higher amounts expected for longer stays, luxury travel, or if no pre-paid arrangements

• Employment letter confirming job will be held upon return

• Enrollment in studies to resume after trip
• Community involvement: club memberships, volunteer roles, religious affiliations

---CHUNK: Australia_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_11---
## Australia - Tourist Visa

; book after application submission if requested

=== VISA CONDITIONS (IF GRANTED) ===
8101 – NO WORK: Cannot engage in work for pay or reward in Australia
8201 – MAX 3 MONTHS STUDY: Can undertake study or training for max 3 months only
8503 – NO FURTHER STAY: Cannot apply for most other visas while in Australia (if this condition is imposed)
8558 – MAX 12 MONTHS IN 18 MONTH PERIOD: Cannot stay more than 12 months in any rolling 18-month period

---CHUNK: Australia_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_12---
## Australia - Tourist Visa

re than 12 months in any rolling 18-month period

=== APPLICATION PROCESS ===
1. Create ImmiAccount: https://online.immi.gov.au
2. Complete Visitor Visa (subclass 600) application form
3. Upload supporting documents (English or certified translation)
4. Pay Visa Application Charge (AUD 200+) by credit card
5. Attend biometrics appointment if requested
6. Wait for decision; do NOT book non-refundable travel until visa granted
7. If granted: print visa grant notice; carry with passport when traveling

---CHUNK: Australia_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_13---
## Australia - Tourist Visa

grant notice; carry with passport when traveling

=== PROCESSING TIMES & DECISION ===
• Check current times: https://immi.homeaffairs.gov.au/visas/getting-a-visa/visa-processing-times
• Times vary by country, season, application completeness, case officer workload
• Case officer may request additional information via ImmiAccount
• No statutory timeframe for decision on visitor visas
• No right of merits review (Administrative Appeals Tribunal) for visitor visa refusals
• Can reapply with new information if refused

---CHUNK: Australia_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_14---
## Australia - Tourist Visa

ls
• Can reapply with new information if refused

=== ENTRY TO AUSTRALIA ===
• Final admissibility determined by Australian Border Force officer at port of entry
• Must present: passport with visa grant notice, return/onward ticket, proof of funds if requested
• Officer may grant shorter stay than visa validity; date will be stamped in passport
• Must comply with all visa conditions; breaches affect future applications

---CHUNK: Australia_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_15---
## Australia - Tourist Visa

conditions; breaches affect future applications

=== RESTRICTIONS ===
✗ Cannot work in Australia (including freelance, gig economy, remote work for foreign employer if it displaces local worker)
✗ Cannot study for programs >3 months duration
✗ Cannot access Australian public funds (Medicare, welfare, unemployment benefits)
✗ Cannot apply for most other visas while in Australia if condition 8503 is imposed
✗ Overstaying results in exclusion period (typically 3 years) for future visa applications

## Canada - Family Visa

VISA TYPE: Family Sponsorship (Spouse/Partner/Dependent Child)
COUNTRY: Canada
SOURCE: https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/immigrate-canada/family-sponsorship.html
LAST UPDATED: 2024

---CHUNK: Canada_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_1---
## Canada - Family Visa

anada/family-sponsorship.html
LAST UPDATED: 2024

=== SPONSOR ELIGIBILITY ===
SPONSOR MUST:
□ Be at least 18 years old
□ Be a Canadian citizen, permanent resident, or person registered under Canadian Indian Act
□ Live in Canada (citizens abroad may sponsor if proving intent to return; PRs abroad cannot sponsor)
□ Sign undertaking and sponsorship agreement committing to financial support
□ Meet requirements under Immigration and Refugee Protection Act/Regulations

---CHUNK: Canada_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_2---
## Canada - Family Visa

migration and Refugee Protection Act/Regulations

=== INCOME REQUIREMENTS ===
• Generally NO minimum income requirement to sponsor spouse, partner, or dependent child
• Income requirement APPLIES ONLY if:
  - Sponsoring a dependent child who has their own dependent child(ren), OR
  - Sponsoring a spouse/partner who has a dependent child, and that child has dependent child(ren)
• Use Financial Evaluation Form (IMM 1283) to calculate required amount
• Quebec sponsors must meet Quebec's income rules (if applicable)

---CHUNK: Canada_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_3---
## Canada - Family Visa

must meet Quebec's income rules (if applicable)

=== WHO CAN BE SPONSORED ===
SPOUSE:
• Legally married to sponsor
• At least 18 years old
• Any gender
• In genuine relationship (not for immigration purposes only)
• Not inadmissible to Canada

COMMON-LAW PARTNER:
• Lived together continuously in conjugal relationship for at least 1 year
• At least 18 years old
• Genuine relationship, not inadmissible

---CHUNK: Canada_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_4---
## Canada - Family Visa

ars old
• Genuine relationship, not inadmissible

CONJUGAL PARTNER:
• In conjugal relationship for 1+ year
• Unable to live together or marry due to immigration barriers, legal restrictions, or persecution
• At least 18 years old, genuine relationship, not inadmissible

DEPENDENT CHILD:
• Under 22 years old AND not married/common-law, OR
• 22+ if financially dependent due to physical/mental condition
• Must not be inadmissible

---CHUNK: Canada_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_5---

ical/mental condition
• Must not be inadmissible

=== GENUINE RELATIONSHIP PROOF (EXAMPLES) ===
• Marriage certificate + wedding photos
• Joint financial documents (bank accounts, leases, bills, insurance)
• Communication records (calls, messages, emails) over time
• Travel records showing visits
• Letters from family/friends confirming relationship
• Statutory declarations from people who know the couple

---CHUNK: Canada_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_6---

ory declarations from people who know the couple

=== INADMISSIBILITY GROUNDS (SPONSORED PERSON) ===
May be refused if sponsored person has:
✗ Criminal record (severity/rehabilitation considered)
✗ Medical condition posing public health/safety risk OR excessive demand on services
✗ Security concerns (espionage, terrorism, organized crime)
✗ Human rights violations
✗ Misrepresentation (fraud, fake documents)
✗ Previous immigration violations (overstay, unauthorized work)

• Spouse/Common-Law (inside or outside Canada): ~12 months (check IRCC website for updates)

• Quebec applications: Additional time for MIFI assessment

---CHUNK: Canada_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_11---
## Canada - Family Visa

pplications: Additional time for MIFI assessment

=== QUEBEC-SPECIFIC PROCESS ===
1. IRCC assesses sponsor eligibility first
2. If approved, IRCC invites sponsor to apply to MIFI (Quebec)
3. MIFI issues Certificat de sélection du Québec (CSQ) if approved
4. Federal stage resumes for final PR decision
• Note: MIFI has cap on undertakings for spouse/partner/dependent child 18+ until June 25, 2026
• Do NOT submit Quebec undertaking until invited by IRCC

---CHUNK: Canada_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_12---
## Canada - Family Visa

submit Quebec undertaking until invited by IRCC

=== SUPER VISA ALTERNATIVE (PARENTS/GRANDPARENTS) ===
If sponsorship backlog is long, consider Super Visa:
• Multiple-entry visa valid up to 10 years
• Allows stays up to 5 years per entry
• Requirements: Child/grandchild in Canada meets income threshold, private medical insurance ($100k coverage), medical exam
• Faster processing; does not lead to PR directly but allows extended visits

---CHUNK: Canada_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_13---
## Canada - Family Visa

t lead to PR directly but allows extended visits

=== POST-APPROVAL ===
• Sponsored person becomes permanent resident upon entry to Canada
• Sponsor's undertaking lasts 3 years from date PR is granted (for spouse/partner)
• Sponsored person has right to work, study, access healthcare immediately
• Conditional permanent residence (2-year cohabitation requirement) was removed in 2017

---CHUNK: Canada_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_14---
## Canada - Family Visa

ar cohabitation requirement) was removed in 2017

=== APPEAL RIGHTS ===
• If application refused, sponsor may appeal to Immigration Appeal Division (IAD) if:
  - Refusal was not due to inadmissibility (serious criminality, security, human rights violations), AND
  - Sponsor is Canadian citizen or PR
• Appeal must be filed within 30 days of refusal notice

## Canada - Student Visa

## Canada - Student Visa
### Source: Canada_Student.txt

REQUIREMENTS:
- Acceptance letter from designated learning institution
- Prove sufficient funds for tuition and living
- Be law-abiding citizen with no criminal record
- Be in good health

REQUIRED DOCUMENTS:
- Valid passport
- Letter of acceptance
- Proof of financial support (CAD $10,000+/year)

---CHUNK: China_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_1---
## China - Family Visa

https://www.visaforchina.org
LAST UPDATED: 2024

=== OVERVIEW ===
• S1 Visa: For long-term family reunion (>180 days) with foreign nationals working/studying in China
• S2 Visa: For short-term family visits (≤180 days) with foreign nationals or Chinese citizens
• S1 Visa holders must convert to Residence Permit within 30 days of entry
• Sponsored by family member legally residing in China (foreigner with Work/Student Residence Permit OR Chinese citizen)

---CHUNK: China_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_2---
## China - Family Visa

ork/Student Residence Permit OR Chinese citizen)

=== ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA ===
SPONSOR IN CHINA MUST:
□ Be a foreign national holding valid Work (Z) or Student (X1) Residence Permit in China, OR
□ Be a Chinese citizen with household registration (hukou) or valid Chinese ID
□ Have stable residence and sufficient financial means to support visiting family member
□ Not have adverse immigration or legal history in China

---CHUNK: China_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_3---
## China - Family Visa

ve adverse immigration or legal history in China

ELIGIBLE FAMILY RELATIONSHIPS:
□ Spouse: Legally married to sponsor (marriage certificate required)
□ Children: Unmarried children under 18 of sponsor or sponsor's spouse
□ Parents: Parents of sponsor (for S1 Visa with foreign sponsor; more flexible for Chinese citizen sponsor)
□ Other relatives: Siblings, grandparents, etc. may qualify for S2 Visa on case-by-case basis

---CHUNK: China_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_4---
## China - Family Visa

c. may qualify for S2 Visa on case-by-case basis

NON-ELIGIBLE RELATIONSHIPS:
✗ Unmarried partners, fiancé(e)s (unless legally recognized in home country)
✗ Adult married children (unless financially dependent and exceptional circumstances)
✗ Distant relatives without proof of close relationship/dependency

#### S1 VISA (LONG-TERM FAMILY REUNION >180 DAYS)
MANDATORY DOCUMENTS:
□ Completed online visa application form (https://cova.cs.mfa.gov.cn)
□ Printed and signed application form with recent passport photo attached:
  - Photo specs: 48mm x 33mm, white background, frontal view
□ Original passport (valid 6+ months beyond intended stay, 2 blank pages)
□ Photocopy of passport biodata page
□ Invitation letter from sponsor in China:

  - If sponsor is Chinese citizen: Copy of Chinese ID (front/back) or passport + household registration proof
  - Letter content: Relationship to applicant, purpose/duration of visit, accommodation details, financial support commitment
□ Proof of family relationship:
  - Spouse: Attested marriage certificate (translated to Chinese if not in Chinese/English)
  - Children: Attested birth certificate showing parentage
  - Parents: Birth certificate of sponsor + proof of relationship
□ For foreign sponsor: Copy of sponsor's Work Permit/Admission Notice + institution/employer letter confirming relationship

## China - Family Visa

s Chinese ID copy + household registration proof

=== APPLICATION PROCESS ===
STEP-BY-STEP:
1. Sponsor in China prepares invitation letter + supporting documents (ID/Residence Permit copy, relationship proof)
2. Applicant completes online visa application at https://cova.cs.mfa.gov.cn
3. Print, sign, and gather all required documents (originals + photocopies)
4. Submit application at Chinese Embassy/Consulate or CVASC (appointment required)
5. Pay visa fee as directed (varies by nationality)
6. Processing time: 4 business days standard; expedited options available
7. Upon approval: Collect passport with S1/S2 Visa sticker
8. For S1 Visa: Enter China within visa validity; convert to Residence Permit within 30 days of entry

---CHUNK: China_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_10---
## China - Family Visa

vert to Residence Permit within 30 days of entry

CONVERTING S1 VISA TO RESIDENCE PERMIT:
• Must apply at local Exit-Entry Administration Bureau of Public Security within 30 days of entry
• Required documents:
  - Passport with S1 Visa + entry stamp
  - Sponsor's documents: Chinese ID or foreign passport + valid Residence Permit
  - Proof of family relationship (original + copy)
  - Temporary Registration Form of Accommodation (from hotel, dorm, or local police station)
  - Sponsor's proof of residence and financial support
  - Application form + recent photo
• Processing: 7-15 working days; applicant receives Residence Permit sticker in passport
• Residence Permit validity: Typically matches sponsor's Residence Permit validity or up to 1-2 years

PROCESSING TIMES:
• S1/S2 Visa application abroad: 4 business days standard; 2-3 days express; 1 day rush
• Residence Permit conversion in China (S1 only): 7-15 working days
• Peak seasons (Chinese New Year, summer holidays): Apply 2-3 weeks in advance

=== VISA VALIDITY & EXTENSION ===
S2 VISA (SHORT-TERM):
• Validity: Typically 3-12 months from date of issue (depending on nationality/reciprocity)

• Generally NOT extendable within China except in exceptional circumstances (medical emergency, force majeure)

---CHUNK: China_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_15---
## China - Family Visa

circumstances (medical emergency, force majeure)

S1 VISA + RESIDENCE PERMIT (LONG-TERM):
• Initial Residence Permit validity: Typically matches sponsor's Residence Permit validity or up to 1-2 years
• Multiple-entry allowed; holder can travel in/out of China freely during validity
• Extension: Apply at local Exit-Entry Administration Bureau at least 30 days before expiry
  - Required: Updated sponsor documents, continued proof of relationship/financial support, accommodation proof
  - Processing: 7-15 working days; extension granted for remaining validity of sponsor's status

---CHUNK: China_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_16---
## China - Family Visa

anted for remaining validity of sponsor's status

DEPENDENCY TERMINATION:
• If sponsor's status ends (Residence Permit expiry/cancellation, Chinese citizen sponsor moves abroad):
  - Dependent's S1 Residence Permit becomes invalid simultaneously
  - Dependent has 30-day grace period to:
    • Secure independent visa status (e.g., Work/Student Visa), OR
    • Depart China
• Failure to regularize status may result in overstay penalties

STUDY RIGHTS:
• Dependents on S1/S2 Visa CAN enroll in Chinese educational institutions:
  - Schools: No additional visa required for minor children
  - Universities: May continue on S1/S2 Visa for full-time study if course duration ≤ visa validity
  - If course duration exceeds S1/S2 validity: Must apply for Student Visa (X1/X2) change of status

ademic credit may be permitted with PSB approval

=== WORK RIGHTS FOR STUDENT VISA HOLDERS ===
PART-TIME WORK/INTERNSHIPS:
• X1/X2 Visa holders ARE PERMITTED to undertake part-time work/internships with prior approval:

  - Work must be related to field of study or for practical training
  - Maximum 20 hours/week during academic term; full-time during vacations
  - Cannot take up full-time employment without changing to Work Visa (Z)

---CHUNK: China_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_1---
## China - Tourist Visa

https://www.visaforchina.org
LAST UPDATED: 2024

=== OVERVIEW ===
• L Visa: For tourism, family visits, or other private affairs
• Single-entry, double-entry, or multiple-entry options available
• Validity: 3 months to 10 years (depending on nationality, reciprocity, and applicant profile)
• Duration of stay per entry: Typically 30-90 days (specified on visa sticker)
• Application via Chinese Embassy/Consulate or authorized Visa Application Service Center (CVASC)

---CHUNK: China_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_2---
## China - Tourist Visa

thorized Visa Application Service Center (CVASC)

=== ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA ===
APPLICANT MUST:
□ Hold passport valid for at least 6 months beyond intended stay, with at least 2 blank visa pages
□ Demonstrate genuine tourism/family visit purpose with supporting documentation
□ Possess confirmed round-trip flight itinerary and accommodation bookings
□ Have sufficient financial means to cover stay in China
□ Not be of Pakistani origin or hold Pakistani passport without special clearance (case-by-case)
□ Not have adverse immigration history with China or other countries

---CHUNK: China_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_3---
## China - Tourist Visa

mmigration history with China or other countries

=== DOCUMENT REQUIREMENTS ===
MANDATORY DOCUMENTS:
□ Completed online visa application form (https://cova.cs.mfa.gov.cn)
□ Printed and signed application form with recent passport photo attached:
  - Photo specs: 48mm x 33mm, white background, frontal view, no glasses/headwear (except religious)
□ Original passport (valid 6+ months, 2+ blank pages)
□ Photocopy of passport biodata page and previous Chinese visas (if applicable)
□ Proof of legal residence in country of application (if not citizen): visa, residence permit, green card
□ Round-trip flight itinerary or confirmed booking (not necessarily paid ticket)
□ Hotel reservations or invitation letter from host in China:
  - If staying with host: Invitation letter + host's Chinese ID/residence permit copy + proof of relationship

---CHUNK: China_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_4---
## China - Tourist Visa

ID/residence permit copy + proof of relationship

ADDITIONAL DOCUMENTS (MAY BE REQUESTED):
□ Bank statements (last 3-6 months) showing sufficient funds (~USD 100-150/day recommended)
□ Travel itinerary detailing cities/sites to visit
□ For group tours: Confirmation letter from licensed travel agency
□ For previous China visa holders: Copies of previous visas/entry stamps

---CHUNK: China_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_5---
## China - Tourist Visa

a holders: Copies of previous visas/entry stamps

=== APPLICATION PROCESS ===
STEP-BY-STEP:
1. Complete online application at https://cova.cs.mfa.gov.cn (China Online Visa Application)
2. Print, sign, and attach photo to application form
3. Gather all required documents (originals + photocopies)
4. Submit application at:
   • Chinese Embassy/Consulate in country of residence, OR
   • Authorized Chinese Visa Application Service Center (CVASC): https://www.visaforchina.org
   • Appointment required at most locations; book via CVASC website
5. Pay visa fee as directed (varies by nationality, entry type, processing speed)
6. Processing time: 4 business days standard; expedited options available (2-3 days, 1 day)
7. Collect passport with visa sticker or receive via courier if service available

---CHUNK: China_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_6---
## China - Tourist Visa

cker or receive via courier if service available

PROCESSING TIMES:
• Standard: 4 business days from submission
• Express: 2-3 business days (additional fee)
• Rush: 1 business day (additional fee, subject to approval)
• Peak seasons (Chinese New Year, summer): Apply 2-3 weeks in advance

cn | https://www.fmprc.gov.cn

=== OVERVIEW ===
• Z Visa: For foreigners taking up employment or commercial performance in China
• Single-entry visa valid for 30 days from entry; must convert to Residence Permit within 30 days
• Sponsored by Chinese employer; requires Work Permit Notice from Ministry of Human Resources and Social Security (MOHRSS) or State Administration of Foreign Experts Affairs (SAFEA)
• Mandatory registration with local Public Security Bureau within 24 hours of arrival

---CHUNK: China_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_2---
## China - Work Visa

ublic Security Bureau within 24 hours of arrival

=== ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA ===
APPLICANT MUST:
□ Have valid job offer/employment contract from Chinese employer registered to hire foreigners
□ Possess bachelor's degree or higher OR 2+ years relevant work experience (for most categories)
□ Be aged 18-60 (men) or 18-55 (women); exceptions for high-level talent
□ Pass health examination at authorized facility (report valid for 6 months)
□ Have no criminal record in home country or China
□ Not be of Pakistani origin or hold Pakistani passport without special clearance (case-by-case)

---CHUNK: China_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_3---

assport without special clearance (case-by-case)

✓ Executives, managers, technical experts assigned to Chinese entity
✓ Teachers/faculty at recognized Chinese educational institutions
✓ Skilled professionals in IT, engineering, finance, healthcare, education
✓ Artists, performers, athletes with commercial contracts
✓ High-level talent (Category A) under China's foreign talent recruitment programs

---CHUNK: China_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_4---

nder China's foreign talent recruitment programs

NON-QUALIFYING CATEGORIES:
✗ Routine administrative/clerical staff without specialized skills
✗ Short-term consultants (<90 days; may use M/Business Visa)
✗ Self-employed freelancers serving Chinese clients (requires different authorization)
✗ Volunteers, interns without formal employment contract and Work Permit

thout formal employment contract and Work Permit

=== DOCUMENT REQUIREMENTS ===
MANDATORY DOCUMENTS:
□ Completed online visa application form (https://cova.cs.mfa.gov.cn)
□ Printed and signed application form with recent passport photo attached
□ Original passport (valid 6+ months beyond intended stay, 2 blank pages)
□ Photocopy of passport biodata page
□ Work Permit Notice (original + copy):
  - Issued by Chinese employer via MOHRSS/SAFEA online system
  - Contains unique permit number, employer details, position, validity
□ Health Examination Certificate:
  - Conducted at authorized facility in home country or China
  - Report valid for 6 months; must include chest X-ray, blood tests, physical exam
□ No Criminal Record Certificate:
  - Issued by home country authorities within last 6 months
  - Must be authenticated/legalized for use in China
□ Educational/Professional Qualifications:
  - Bachelor's degree or higher (or 2+ years experience for certain categories)
  - Degrees issued outside China must be authenticated by Chinese Embassy/Consulate
□ Employment contract or official invitation letter from Chinese employer:
  - On company letterhead, signed, with company seal
  - Details: position, salary, duration, responsibilities, company registration info

ion, responsibilities, company registration info

s, publications, patents, recommendation letters

=== APPLICATION PROCESS ===
STEP-BY-STEP:
1. Chinese employer applies for Work Permit Notice via MOHRSS/SAFEA online system
2. Upon approval: Employer sends original Work Permit Notice to applicant abroad
3. Applicant completes online visa application at https://cova.cs.mfa.gov.cn
4. Print, sign, and gather all required documents (originals + photocopies)
5. Submit application at Chinese Embassy/Consulate or CVASC (appointment required)
6. Pay visa fee as directed (varies by nationality)
7. Processing time: 4 business days standard; expedited options available
8. Upon approval: Collect passport with Z Visa sticker (single-entry, 30-day validity from entry)
9. Enter China within Z Visa validity; convert to Residence Permit within 30 days of entry

---CHUNK: China_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_8---
## China - Work Visa

vert to Residence Permit within 30 days of entry

CONVERTING Z VISA TO RESIDENCE PERMIT:
• Must apply at local Exit-Entry Administration Bureau of Public Security within 30 days of entry
• Required documents:
  - Passport with Z Visa + entry stamp
  - Work Permit (original, issued after entry)
  - Health examination report (if not already submitted)
  - Temporary Registration Form of Accommodation (from hotel or local police station)
  - Employer's business license + foreigner employment registration certificate
  - Application form + recent photo
• Processing: 7-15 working days; applicant receives Residence Permit sticker in passport
• Residence Permit validity: Typically 1 year, renewable; matches Work Permit validity

---CHUNK: China_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_9---
## China - Work Visa

1 year, renewable; matches Work Permit validity

PROCESSING TIMES:
• Z Visa application abroad: 4 business days standard; 2-3 days express; 1 day rush
• Residence Permit conversion in China: 7-15 working days
• Work Permit Notice application by employer: 5-15 working days (varies by city/category)

• USA citizens: ~USD 140-180

CATEGORY A (HIGH-LEVEL TALENT):
• Eligibility: Senior executives, PhD holders, high-salary earners (≥2x local average), award winners, entrepreneurs
• Benefits: Fast-track Work Permit processing, longer validity (up to 5 years), family dependents eligible for longer permits
• Documentation: Enhanced proof of achievements, awards, publications, patents

---CHUNK: China_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_13---
## China - Work Visa

f of achievements, awards, publications, patents

CATEGORY B (PROFESSIONAL TALENT):
• Eligibility: Bachelor's degree + 2 years experience, mid-level professionals, teachers, skilled technicians
• Standard processing timeline and validity (typically 1 year)
• Most common category for foreign employees

---CHUNK: China_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_14---
## China - Work Visa

ar)
• Most common category for foreign employees

CATEGORY C (OTHER FOREIGN WORKERS):
• Eligibility: Seasonal workers, interns, short-term contractors (subject to quotas/restrictions)
• More stringent approval process; limited validity (≤1 year)
• Subject to labor market testing and quota controls

=== RESIDENCE PERMIT VALIDITY & RENEWAL ===
INITIAL VALIDITY:
• Typically 1 year, matching Work Permit validity
• Multiple-entry allowed; holder can travel in/out of China freely during validity

---CHUNK: China_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_15---
## China - Work Visa

an travel in/out of China freely during validity

RENEWAL PROCESS:
• Apply at local Exit-Entry Administration Bureau at least 30 days before expiry
• Required documents:
  - Valid passport and current Residence Permit
  - Renewed Work Permit from employer
  - Updated health examination report (if required; typically every 1-2 years)
  - Temporary Registration Form of Accommodation
  - Employer's updated business license + foreigner employment registration
• Processing: 7-15 working days; applicant may stay in China during processing with acknowledgment receipt
• Renewal granted in 1-year increments; high-level talent (Category A) may receive 2-5 year renewals

---CHUNK: China_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_16---
## China - Work Visa

alent (Category A) may receive 2-5 year renewals

=== FAMILY DEPENDENTS ===
ELIGIBILITY TO SPONSOR FAMILY:
• Z Visa/Residence Permit holders CAN sponsor spouse and unmarried children under 18 for S1/S2 Visa
• Dependents receive visa validity matching primary holder's Residence Permit

DEPENDENT VISA TYPES:
• S1 Visa: For long-term stay (>180 days); convert to Residence Permit within 30 days of entry
• S2 Visa: For short-term visits (≤180 days); no conversion required

---CHUNK: China_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_17---

-term visits (≤180 days); no conversion required

DEPENDENT RIGHTS:
• Spouse: May study or engage in unpaid activities; cannot work without separate Work Permit
• Children: Can enroll in Chinese schools; cannot work without authorization
• All dependents: Must register with local police within 24 hours of arrival; apply for Residence Permit if staying >180 days

apply for Residence Permit if staying >180 days

=== TAX & COMPLIANCE OBLIGATIONS ===
INCOME TAX:
• Foreign employees are tax residents if stay in China exceeds 183 days in a calendar year
• Must obtain Tax Identification Number from local tax bureau
• Employer typically withholds Individual Income Tax (IIT); file annual tax reconciliation

---CHUNK: China_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_19---
## China - Work Visa

Income Tax (IIT); file annual tax reconciliation

SOCIAL INSURANCE:
• Foreign employees in China generally required to contribute to social insurance (pension, medical, unemployment, work injury, maternity)
• Exemptions possible under bilateral social security agreements (e.g., with Germany, South Korea, Canada)
• Contribution rates vary by city; typically 10-20% of salary shared between employer/employee

---CHUNK: China_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_20---

0-20% of salary shared between employer/employee

LABOR LAW COMPLIANCE:
• Employment must comply with Chinese Labor Contract Law: minimum wage, working hours (max 44 hrs/week), leave entitlements
• Foreign employees have same rights as Chinese employees under most labor statutes
• Disputes resolved via local labor arbitration committees

---CHUNK: China_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_21---

resolved via local labor arbitration committees

=== VISA/PERMIT CANCELLATION & EXIT PROCEDURES ===
EMPLOYMENT TERMINATION:
• If employment ends before permit expiry: Employer must cancel Work Permit and notify authorities within 10 days
• Residence Permit holder has 30-day grace period to:
  - Secure new employment and transfer Work Permit sponsorship, OR
  - Change visa status (e.g., to S2/Tourist Visa), OR
  - Depart China

==== LONG-STAY VISA (GENERAL) ====
WHEN REQUIRED:
• Any stay in France exceeding 90 days within 180-day period
• Applies regardless of nationality (even visa-exempt nationals need long-stay visa for >90 days)

empt nationals need long-stay visa for >90 days)

## France - Tourist Visa

VISA TYPE: France Short-Stay & Long-Stay Visitor Visas (Tourism/Private Stay/Medical)
COUNTRY: France / Schengen Area
SOURCE: https://france-visas.gouv.fr/en/web/france-visas/

---CHUNK: France_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_1---
## France - Tourist Visa

.gouv.fr/en/web/france-visas/
LAST UPDATED: 2024

=== OVERVIEW ===
• Tourism/private stay: No professional activity permitted (except Working Holiday eligible nationals)
• Short-stay (≤90 days in 180-day period): Uniform Schengen Visa (Type C) or French national visa
• Long-stay (>90 days): Long-stay visitor visa (VLS-TS) serving as residence permit
• Medical care visa: Short-stay visa for treatment; does not cover costs via French health system
• Airport transit: Check if Airport Transit Visa (ATV) required based on nationality

---CHUNK: France_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_2---
## France - Tourist Visa

Transit Visa (ATV) required based on nationality

=== ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA ===

---CHUNK: France_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_3---

sed on nationality

=== ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA ===

#### SHORT-STAY VISA (≤90 DAYS)
APPLICANT MUST:
□ Have nationality requiring visa for France/Schengen (check France-Visas wizard)
□ Intend stay ≤90 days within any 180-day period across Schengen Area
□ Not engage in professional activity during stay
□ Prove sufficient financial resources for duration of stay + return travel
□ Hold valid travel insurance (€30,000 minimum coverage)
□ Have confirmed accommodation for entire stay
□ Possess passport valid 3+ months beyond intended departure, issued <10 years ago
□ Provide proof of intent to return to country of residence

---CHUNK: France_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_4---
## France - Tourist Visa

roof of intent to return to country of residence

FINANCIAL MEANS (GUIDELINE):
• €120/day if no pre-paid accommodation
• €65/day if hotel/pre-paid accommodation confirmed
• €32.50/day for minors traveling with family
• Acceptable proof: Bank statements (3 months), cash, traveler's checks, international credit cards

insurer; French policies accepted automatically

=== APPLICATION PROCESS ===
1. CHECK REQUIREMENT: Use France-Visas wizard https://france-visas.gouv.fr
2. COMPLETE ONLINE APPLICATION: Via France-Visas portal
3. BOOK APPOINTMENT: At Visa Application Centre (VAC) or French Consulate
4. ATTEND APPOINTMENT:
   • Submit documents in required order
   • Provide biometrics (fingerprints + photo) if aged 12+
   • Pay visa fee
5. AWAIT DECISION: Typically 15 calendar days (up to 45 for complex cases)
6. COLLECT PASSPORT: With visa sticker if granted

## France - Work Visa

VISA TYPE: France Young Professional, Working Holiday & Long-Stay Visas
COUNTRY: France / Schengen Area / French Overseas Territories

=== VISA CATEGORIES OVERVIEW ===

---CHUNK: France_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_1---
## France - Work Visa

UPDATED: 2024

=== VISA CATEGORIES OVERVIEW ===

#### YOUNG PROFESSIONAL EXCHANGE VISA
PURPOSE: Professional, linguistic, or cultural development through work placement in France
ELIGIBILITY:
□ Applicant's country has bilateral agreement with France (check "Special features" for your country)
□ Already employed or recently graduated in home country
□ Age limit per agreement: typically 18-30 or 18-35 years
□ Secure job offer/training placement with French company
□ Employer submits work permit application to OFII Direction Territoriale

---CHUNK: France_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_2---
## France - Work Visa

ermit application to OFII Direction Territoriale

APPLICATION PROCESS:
1. Employer files work permit application with OFII in France
2. Applicant prepares file:
   • Valid passport (valid 3+ months beyond intended stay)
   • Biometric photos (35x45 mm)
   • Employment contract or training agreement
   • Proof of qualifications (diplomas, CV)
   • Proof of financial means (~€2,500 minimum)
   • Health insurance covering entire stay
3. Submit complete file to OFII or its delegation in home country
4. OFII forwards to Consulate for visa examination
5. If granted: Long-stay VLS-TS visa with "jeune professionnel" mention
6. Validate visa online within 3 months of arrival in France

---CHUNK: France_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_3---
## France - Work Visa

visa online within 3 months of arrival in France

VISA DETAILS:
• Type: Long-stay visa equivalent to residence permit (VLS-TS)
• Validity: Matches employment/training duration (max 12 months typically)
• Work rights: Authorized to work only for sponsoring employer
• Travel: Can travel within Schengen Area under 90/180-day rule
• Renewal: Must apply for residence permit at Prefecture if extending stay

• No fee for appeal; decision typically 1-2 months
• Alternative: Reapply with stronger, targeted documentation

90/180-DAY RULE:

=== OVERVIEW ===
• Entry (X) Visa for dependents of foreign nationals legally residing in India on long-term visas (Employment, Student, Research, Project, etc.)
• For: Spouse, unmarried children under 25, dependent parents (in exceptional circumstances)

• NOT for independent travel/tourism; dependent status tied to primary visa holder

=== APPLICATION PROCESS ===
STEP-BY-STEP:
1. Primary visa holder ensures their own visa/FRRO registration is valid and up-to-date
2. Dependent completes online application at https://indianvisaonline.gov.in
3. Print, sign, and gather all required documents
4. Submit application + documents at:
   • Indian Embassy/Consulate in dependent's country of residence, OR
   • Authorized VFS Global center (appointment required in many locations)
5. Pay visa fee as directed (varies by nationality and validity)
6. Processing time: 5-15 working days (may be longer if relationship verification required)
7. Upon approval: Collect passport with Entry (X) Visa sticker
8. Enter India; register with FRRO/FRO within 14 days if stay >180 days

## India - Student Visa

.gov.in | https://frro.gov.in

=== OVERVIEW ===
• For foreigners admitted to recognized educational institutions in India for full-time academic programs
• Covers: University degrees, diploma courses, research programs, language studies, yoga/ayurveda courses at recognized institutions
• Validity: Duration of course + 1 year (or as specified by institution), extendable in India
• Mandatory registration with FRRO/FRO within 14 days of arrival if stay >180 days

---CHUNK: India_Student_20260315_214737_chunk_2---
## India - Student Visa

/FRO within 14 days of arrival if stay >180 days

=== ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA ===
APPLICANT MUST:
□ Have admission offer from recognized Indian educational institution (UGC/AICTE/ICMR/other recognized body)
□ Be enrolled in full-time academic program (part-time/distance learning not eligible for Student Visa)
□ Hold passport valid for at least 6 months beyond intended course duration
□ Demonstrate sufficient financial resources to cover tuition + living expenses
□ Not be of Pakistani origin or hold Pakistani passport (special clearance required)

Pakistani passport (special clearance required)

RECOGNIZED INSTITUTIONS:
• Universities recognized by University Grants Commission (UGC): https://www.ugc.ac.in
• Technical institutions recognized by AICTE: https://www.aicte-india.org
• Medical institutions recognized by NMC: https://www.nmc.org.in
• Other recognized bodies: ICMR, ICAR, BCI, etc.
• Private institutions must have valid recognition/approval from relevant authority

QUALIFYING PROGRAMS:
✓ Bachelor's, Master's, PhD degrees at recognized universities
✓ Diploma/certificate courses (minimum 6 months duration) at recognized institutions
✓ Research fellowships, post-doctoral programs
✓ Language studies (Hindi, Sanskrit, etc.) at recognized institutes
✓ Yoga, Ayurveda, traditional medicine courses at recognized institutions

=== DOCUMENT REQUIREMENTS ===
MANDATORY DOCUMENTS:
□ Completed online application form (https://indianvisaonline.gov.in)
□ Original passport (valid 6+ months beyond intended course duration, 2 blank pages)
□ Two recent passport-sized photographs (2x2 inches, white background)
□ Admission letter from recognized Indian institution (on letterhead, signed):
  - Course name, duration, start/end dates
  - Tuition fees and payment schedule
  - Institution's recognition/accreditation details
□ Proof of financial means:
  - Bank statements (last 6 months) showing sufficient funds, OR
  - Scholarship award letter, OR
  - Sponsorship letter + sponsor's financial documents + proof of relationship
□ Educational qualifications: Attested copies of prior degrees/diplomas, transcripts
□ For research programs: Research proposal, supervisor acceptance letter, institutional approval

□ Medical fitness certificate (especially for long-term stays)
□ Police clearance certificate (for certain nationalities/programs)
□ For minor students (<18): Parental consent letter, guardian details in India
□ For language/yoga courses: Proof of prior study or aptitude (if required by institution)

---CHUNK: India_Student_20260315_214737_chunk_8---
## India - Student Visa

r study or aptitude (if required by institution)

=== APPLICATION PROCESS ===
STEP-BY-STEP:
1. Secure admission from recognized Indian institution; obtain formal admission letter
2. Complete online application at https://indianvisaonline.gov.in
3. Print, sign, and gather all required documents
4. Submit application + documents at:
   • Indian Embassy/Consulate in country of residence, OR
   • Authorized VFS Global center (appointment required in many locations)
5. Pay visa fee as directed (varies by nationality and validity)
6. Processing time: 5-15 working days (longer for certain nationalities/programs)
7. Upon approval: Collect passport with Student Visa sticker
8. Enter India; register with FRRO/FRO within 14 days if stay >180 days

---CHUNK: India_Student_20260315_214737_chunk_9---
## India - Student Visa

r with FRRO/FRO within 14 days if stay >180 days

PROCESSING TIMES:
• Standard cases: 5-10 working days at most Missions
• Cases requiring additional verification (certain nationalities, research programs): 10-20 working days
• Peak seasons (Jun-Aug for academic year start): Apply 3-4 weeks in advance

=== VISA VALIDITY & EXTENSION ===
INITIAL VALIDITY:
• Typically granted for duration of course + 1 year (for post-completion departure preparation)
• Example: 2-year Master's program → Visa valid for 3 years
• Multiple entry allowed; each stay typically up to 180 days

---CHUNK: India_Student_20260315_214737_chunk_12---
## India - Student Visa

ntry allowed; each stay typically up to 180 days

EXTENSION IN INDIA:
• Apply via FRRO/FRO portal (https://frro.gov.in) at least 2 months before expiry
• Required documents:
  - Valid passport and current Student Visa
  - Updated admission letter/continuation certificate from institution
  - Proof of academic progress (transcripts, attendance records)
  - Proof of continued financial support
  - FRRO registration certificate (if previously registered)
• Processing: 2-4 weeks; applicant may stay in India during processing with acknowledgment receipt
• Extension granted for remaining course duration + 1 year

n granted for remaining course duration + 1 year

POST-COMPLETION STAY:
• After course completion, Student Visa remains valid for up to 1 year for:
  - Preparing for departure, OR
  - Pursuing further studies in India (with new admission and visa extension), OR
  - Seeking employment (must change to Employment Visa if job secured)

=== FRRO/FRO REGISTRATION REQUIREMENT ===
MANDATORY REGISTRATION:
• Foreigners on Student Visa staying >180 days continuously MUST register with nearest FRRO/FRO within 14 days of arrival
• Registration is also required if total stay in India exceeds 180 days in a calendar year

---CHUNK: India_Student_20260315_214737_chunk_15---

tay in India exceeds 180 days in a calendar year

REGISTRATION PROCESS:
1. Visit FRRO/FRO portal: https://frro.gov.in
2. Create account and fill registration form
3. Upload required documents:
   - Passport copy (biodata page + visa page)
   - Admission letter, institution details
   - Proof of Indian address (hostel letter, rental agreement, institution letter)
   - Recent photograph
4. Pay registration fee: ~INR 100-500 (varies by duration)
5. Attend in-person appointment at FRRO/FRO office (if required)
6. Receive Registration Certificate (RC) – must carry at all times

---CHUNK: India_Student_20260315_214737_chunk_16---

ation Certificate (RC) – must carry at all times

CONSEQUENCES OF NON-REGISTRATION:
• Fine: INR 1,000-10,000 depending on delay duration
• Difficulty extending visa, obtaining NOC for travel, or accessing other immigration services
• Potential impact on future Indian visa applications

=== WORK RIGHTS FOR STUDENT VISA HOLDERS ===
PART-TIME WORK:
• Student Visa holders ARE PERMITTED to undertake part-time work/internships with prior approval:
  - Must obtain No Objection Certificate (NOC) from institution AND FRRO/FRO
  - Work must be related to field of study or for practical training
  - Maximum 20 hours/week during academic term; full-time during vacations
  - Cannot take up full-time employment without changing to Employment Visa

• Stipend/salary: Permitted; must comply with Indian labor laws and tax regulations

v.in | https://www.mea.gov.in

• Tourist visa for recreation, sightseeing, casual visit to meet friends/relatives, short-duration medical treatment, casual business visit

166+ countries; check eligibility by nationality

=== e-TOURIST VISA (e-Visa) ELIGIBILITY ===
ELIGIBLE NATIONALITIES:
• 166+ countries including USA, UK, Canada, Australia, most EU nations, Japan, Singapore, UAE, etc.
• Full list: https://indianvisaonline.gov.in/evisa/tvoa.html

e-VISA SUB-CATEGORIES & VALIDITY:
1. e-Tourist Visa (30 days):
   • Validity: 30 days from date of arrival
   • Entries: Double entry
   • Fee: USD 25 (varies by nationality)

e entry
   • Fee: USD 25 (varies by nationality)

2. e-Tourist Visa (1 year):
   • Validity: 365 days from date of grant
   • Entries: Multiple entry
   • Max stay per visit: 90 days (180 days for USA/UK/Canada/Japan citizens)

3. e-Tourist Visa (5 years):
   • Validity: 5 years from date of grant
   • Entries: Multiple entry
   • Max stay per visit: 90 days (180 days for USA/UK/Canada/Japan citizens)
   • Fee: USD 80 (varies by nationality)

=== APPLICATION PROCESS ===

#### e-TOURIST VISA (ONLINE)
STEPS:
1. Visit https://indianvisaonline.gov.in/evisa/tvoa.html
2. Fill online application form with personal, passport, travel details
3. Upload passport scan and photograph per specifications
4. Pay visa fee via credit/debit card or PayPal
5. Receive Application ID via email; track status online
6. Processing time: Typically 72 hours (apply at least 4 days before travel)
7. Upon approval: Receive e-Visa via email; print copy to carry while traveling
8. At Indian airport: Present printed e-Visa + passport at dedicated e-Visa immigration counter

---CHUNK: India_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_11---

passport at dedicated e-Visa immigration counter

IMPORTANT e-VISA RULES:
• Apply minimum 4 days before travel; maximum 120 days before travel
• e-Visa is non-extendable and non-convertible to other visa types
• Entry allowed only through 28 designated airports and 5 designated seaports
• Exit can be from any authorized Immigration Check Post in India
• e-Visa holders must carry printed copy + passport with same details used in application

• e-Tourist Visa: No explicit annual limit, but consecutive stays should not appear as de facto residence
• Regular Tourist Visa: Continuous stay beyond 180 days may require registration with FRRO

---CHUNK: Singapor_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_0---
## Singapor - Family Visa

VISA TYPE: Singapore Family Visas (Dependant's Pass, Long-Term Visit Pass, LTVP+)
COUNTRY: Singapore
SOURCE: https://www.mom.gov.sg | https://www.ica.gov.sg
LAST UPDATED: 2024

=== OVERVIEW ===
Singapore offers several passes for family members of foreign professionals, entrepreneurs, and Singapore Citizens/Permanent Residents (SC/PR). The type of pass depends on the sponsor's status and the family relationship.

---CHUNK: Singapor_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_1---
## Singapor - Family Visa

he sponsor's status and the family relationship.

MAIN FAMILY PASS TYPES:
1. Dependant's Pass (DP): For legally married spouses and unmarried children (<21) of Employment Pass (EP), S Pass, or EntrePass holders.
2. Long-Term Visit Pass (LTVP): For common-law spouses, step-children, handicapped children (>21), parents of EP holders, or family of SC/PR.
3. LTVP+ (Enhanced): For spouses of Singapore Citizens with stable income; offers longer validity and work rights.
4. Pre-approved LTVP (for EP holders): High earners can get pre-approval for spouse/parents before they arrive.

---CHUNK: Singapor_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_2---
## Singapor - Family Visa

-approval for spouse/parents before they arrive.

=== 1. DEPENDANT'S PASS (DP) ===
ELIGIBILITY - SPONSOR MUST:
□ Hold a valid Employment Pass (EP), S Pass, or EntrePass.
□ Earn a fixed monthly salary of at least SGD 6,000 (higher for older applications).
□ Work for a well-established, reputable firm in Singapore.

ELIGIBLE FAMILY MEMBERS:
• Legally married spouse.
• Unmarried children under 21 years old (including legally adopted children).

---CHUNK: Singapor_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_3---
## Singapor - Family Visa

years old (including legally adopted children).

KEY BENEFITS:
• Validity: Tied to sponsor's pass validity (up to 2 years initially, renewable).
• Work Rights: DP holders CAN work in Singapore WITHOUT a separate work pass, BUT must obtain a Letter of Consent (LOC) from MOM before starting employment.
• Study: Children can attend schools in Singapore.

---CHUNK: Singapor_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_4---
## Singapor - Family Visa

Study: Children can attend schools in Singapore.

DOCUMENTS REQUIRED:
□ Sponsor's passport and current pass details.
□ Marriage certificate (for spouse).
□ Birth certificates (for children).
□ Adoption papers (if applicable).
□ Recent passport-sized photos.
□ Educational certificates (for spouse applying for LOC).

• Admission is subject to vacancy and MOE guidelines.
• International students pay higher fees than citizens/PRs.
• Children do NOT need a separate Student's Pass if holding DP/LTVP.

## Singapor - Tourist Visa

VISA TYPE: Singapore Entry Visa (Short-Term Business/Social Visit)
COUNTRY: Singapore
SOURCE: https://www.ica.gov.sg/enter-transit-depart/entering-singapore/visa_requirements
LAST UPDATED: 2024

---CHUNK: Singapor_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_1---
## Singapor - Tourist Visa

g-singapore/visa_requirements
LAST UPDATED: 2024

=== OVERVIEW & KEY DEFINITIONS ===
ENTRY VISA DEFINITION:
• Pre-entry permission to travel to and seek entry into Singapore
• Does NOT guarantee entry; final decision made by ICA officer at checkpoint
• Does NOT determine duration of stay; Visit Pass (e-Pass) issued at entry sets stay period
• SG Arrival Card is NOT a visa; separate mandatory requirement for all travelers

---CHUNK: Singapor_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_2---
## Singapor - Tourist Visa

separate mandatory requirement for all travelers

e-PASS DIGITAL NOTIFICATION (FROM 11 MARCH 2022):
• Visit Pass issued digitally via email (no passport endorsement)
• Email sent to address provided in SG Arrival Card submission
• e-Pass indicates: Period of stay granted, last day of stay allowed, conditions
• Must retain e-Pass email; may be requested by authorities during stay

---CHUNK: Singapor_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_3---
## Singapor - Tourist Visa

ail; may be requested by authorities during stay

TRAVEL DOCUMENT HOLDERS REQUIRING VISA:
Afghanistan, Algeria, Armenia, Azerbaijan, Bangladesh, Belarus, Democratic People's Republic of Korea, Egypt, Georgia, India, Iran, Iraq, Jordan, Kazakhstan, Kosovo, Kyrgyzstan, Lebanon, Libya, Mali, Moldova, Morocco, Nigeria, Pakistan, Russia, Somalia, South Sudan, Sudan, Syria, Tajikistan, Tunisia, Turkmenistan, Ukraine, Uzbekistan, Yemen

=== VISA-FREE TRANSIT FACILITY (VFTF) ===
ELIGIBLE NATIONALS:
• Commonwealth of Independent States (CIS) countries
• Georgia, India, Turkmenistan, Ukraine
• Selected PRC document holders: Hong Kong SAR DOI, Macau SAR Travel Permit, PRC Travel Document (non-ordinary passports)

---CHUNK: Singapor_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_16---
## Singapor - Tourist Visa

it, PRC Travel Document (non-ordinary passports)

VFTF CONDITIONS:
□ Must be in transit to/from a third country (NOT returning to country of origin)
□ Must hold valid onward ticket departing Singapore within 96 hours
□ Must meet standard entry requirements: valid passport, sufficient funds, confirmed accommodation
□ Must not have been refused entry to Singapore previously
□ Request VFTF at checkpoint upon arrival; no prior application needed

=== EXTENSION OF STAY (SHORT-TERM VISIT PASS) ===
ELIGIBILITY:
• Must apply BEFORE current Visit Pass expires
• Must have valid reason: medical treatment, family emergency, unforeseen circumstances
• Tourism extensions generally NOT granted unless exceptional circumstances

=== COMPLIANCE & PENALTIES ===
OVERSTAYING CONSEQUENCES:
• Fine: Up to SGD 10,000
• Imprisonment: Up to 6 months
• Caning: For male offenders under 50 (in severe cases)
• Future entry ban: Typically 1-5 years, depending on overstay duration
• Record in immigration system affecting future applications globally

---CHUNK: Singapor_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_24---
## Singapor - Tourist Visa

on system affecting future applications globally

VOLUNTARY DEPARTURE:
• If realize overstay before detection: Report to ICA immediately
• May receive reduced penalty vs. being caught at checkpoint
• Still results in immigration record and potential future restrictions

UNAUTHORIZED EMPLOYMENT:
• Engaging in work without proper work pass is illegal
• Penalties: Fine, imprisonment, deportation, entry ban
• Employers also face penalties for hiring unauthorized workers

• Apply ONLY through official channels: ICA e-Service, authorised visa agents, or Singapore Overseas Missions

## Southkorea - Family Visa

VISA TYPE: South Korea Family Visas (F-1, F-2, F-3, F-4, F-5, F-6)
COUNTRY: South Korea
SOURCE: https://www.hikorea.go.kr | https://overseas.mofa.go.kr
LAST UPDATED: 2024

=== OVERVIEW ===
South Korea offers several family-based residence visas depending on relationship to Korean citizen or foreign resident:

---CHUNK: Southkorea_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_1---
## Southkorea - Family Visa

ationship to Korean citizen or foreign resident:

• F-1: Visiting/Temporary Stay (short-term family visits)
• F-2: Long-term residence (for spouses/children of Korean citizens or permanent residents)
• F-3: Dependent Visa (for family of foreign residents on E/D visas)
• F-4: Overseas Korean Visa (for ethnic Koreans with foreign citizenship)
• F-5: Permanent Residence (after meeting long-term residence criteria)
• F-6: Marriage Immigrant Visa (for foreign spouses of Korean citizens)

nt Visa (for foreign spouses of Korean citizens)

This file focuses on F-3 (Dependent) and F-6 (Marriage Immigrant) as most common for family reunification.

igrant) as most common for family reunification.

=== F-3 DEPENDENT VISA (FOR FAMILY OF FOREIGN RESIDENTS) ===
ELIGIBILITY:
□ Primary visa holder must have valid E (work), D (student), or other long-term visa with ARC
□ Applicant must be spouse or unmarried child under 20 of primary holder
□ Primary holder must demonstrate sufficient financial means to support dependent
□ Accommodation in Korea must meet minimum standards

---CHUNK: Southkorea_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_4---
## Southkorea - Family Visa

commodation in Korea must meet minimum standards

DOCUMENT REQUIREMENTS:
□ Completed visa application form
□ Recent passport-sized photograph (3.5cm x 4.5cm, white background)
□ Original passport (valid 6+ months)
□ Photocopy of passport biodata page
□ Primary holder's ARC copy + passport copy
□ Proof of relationship:
  - Spouse: Attested marriage certificate (apostilled + Korean translation)
  - Child: Attested birth certificate showing parentage (apostilled + Korean translation)
□ Primary holder's proof of financial means: Employment contract, bank statements, tax certificate
□ Proof of accommodation in Korea: Rental agreement, dorm confirmation, or property deed

l agreement, dorm confirmation, or property deed

APPLICATION PROCESS:
• If applying abroad: Submit at Korean Embassy/Consulate with primary holder's documents
• If applying in Korea: Submit at local Immigration Office with primary holder present
• Processing: 5-7 business days abroad; 2-4 weeks in Korea
• Fee: ~USD 30-60 (varies by nationality)

Korea

=== F-6 MARRIAGE IMMIGRANT VISA (FOR FOREIGN SPOUSES OF KOREAN CITIZENS) ===
ELIGIBILITY:
□ Legally married to Korean citizen (marriage registered in Korea)
□ Marriage must be genuine (not for immigration purposes)
□ Korean spouse must meet minimum income/housing requirements to support foreign spouse
□ Applicant must pass basic Korean language/culture interview (at Embassy or Immigration)

## Southkorea - Family Visa

al documents to demonstrate ongoing relationship

APPLICATION PROCESS:
STEP-BY-STEP:
1. Register marriage in Korea (if married abroad): Submit apostilled marriage certificate to Korean Embassy for registration
2. Korean spouse prepares financial/accommodation documentation
3. Applicant completes visa application at Korean Embassy/Consulate
4. Attend interview (if required) to assess relationship genuineness and basic Korean knowledge
5. Submit application + documents
6. Pay visa fee (~USD 30-60)
7. Processing: 2-4 weeks standard; longer if additional verification required
8. Upon approval: Collect passport with F-6 Visa sticker (single-entry, 90-day validity)
9. Enter Korea; apply for ARC at Immigration Office within 90 days

---CHUNK: Southkorea_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_11---
## Southkorea - Family Visa

ply for ARC at Immigration Office within 90 days

OBTAINING ALIEN REGISTRATION CARD (ARC):
• Must apply at local Immigration Office within 90 days of entry
• Required documents:
  - Passport with F-6 Visa + entry stamp
  - Marriage certificate (original + copy)
  - Korean spouse's family registry + ID copy
  - Proof of address in Korea
  - Recent photo + application form + fee (~KRW 30,000)
• Processing: Typically issued same day or within 2-3 weeks
• ARC validity: Initially 1-2 years; renewable based on continued marriage/residence

---CHUNK: Southkorea_Family_20260315_214737_chunk_12---
## Southkorea - Family Visa

renewable based on continued marriage/residence

VISA VALIDITY & RENEWAL:
• Initial ARC validity: Typically 1-2 years
• Renewal: Apply at Immigration Office at least 1 month before expiry
  - Required: Continued proof of marriage, Korean spouse's financial/accommodation proof
  - Processing: 2-4 weeks
• After 2 years of continuous residence on F-6: May apply for F-5 Permanent Residence

✓ Korean language/culture integration support programs available

=== PATHWAY TO PERMANENT RESIDENCE (F-5) ===
ELIGIBILITY FOR F-5 (PERMANENT RESIDENCE):
□ Hold F-6 Visa for at least 2 years of continuous residence in Korea
□ Pass basic Korean language test (TOPIK Level 2 or higher) OR complete government integration program
□ Demonstrate basic knowledge of Korean culture/society
□ Meet income requirement: Annual household income ≥ ~KRW 20-25 million OR asset proof
□ No criminal record in Korea or home country

of

• Apply at local Immigration Office
• Required documents:
  - Valid passport and current F-6 ARC
  - Marriage certificate + Korean spouse's family registry
  - TOPIK score certificate or integration program completion certificate
  - Income/asset proof
  - Criminal record check
  - Application form + fee (~KRW 200,000)
• Processing: 2-3 months
• If approved: Receive F-5 ARC with indefinite validity (renewable every 5 years for card re-issuance)

## Southkorea - Student Visa

| https://overseas.mofa.go.kr
LAST UPDATED: 2024

=== OVERVIEW ===
• D-2 Visa: For foreigners enrolled in degree programs (Bachelor's, Master's, PhD) at recognized Korean universities
• D-4 Visa: For language training, non-degree courses, exchange programs (≤2 years)
• Sponsored by Korean educational institution; requires Certificate of Admission + Visa Issuance Confirmation
• Mandatory registration with Immigration within 90 days of arrival; Alien Registration Card (ARC) required

---CHUNK: Southkorea_Student_20260315_214737_chunk_2---
## Southkorea - Student Visa

arrival; Alien Registration Card (ARC) required

=== ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA ===
APPLICANT MUST:
□ Hold passport valid for at least 6 months beyond intended study period
□ Have formal admission offer from recognized Korean educational institution (university, college, language school)
□ Demonstrate sufficient financial resources to cover tuition + living expenses in Korea
□ Meet academic/language requirements for intended program
□ Pass health examination at authorized facility (for long-term stays)
□ Not have adverse immigration history with Korea or other countries

=== DOCUMENT REQUIREMENTS ===

#### D-2 VISA (DEGREE PROGRAMS)
MANDATORY DOCUMENTS:
□ Completed visa application form (https://www.visa.go.kr)
□ Recent passport-sized photograph (3.5cm x 4.5cm, white background)
□ Original passport (valid 6+ months beyond intended study)
□ Photocopy of passport biodata page
□ Certificate of Admission from Korean institution (original + copy):
  - On official letterhead, signed, with institution seal
  - Details: program name, duration, start/end dates, tuition fees
□ Visa Issuance Confirmation (original + copy):
  - Issued by institution via Hi Korea portal
  - Contains unique confirmation number, student details, program info
□ Proof of financial means:
  - Bank statements (last 6 months) showing sufficient funds (~USD 10,000-20,000 recommended for 1 year)
  - Scholarship award letter, OR
  - Sponsorship letter + sponsor's financial documents + proof of relationship
□ Highest academic degree certificate + transcript (apostilled/legalized if issued outside Korea)
□ Korean language proficiency proof (if required by program): TOPIK score, institutional test results

=== APPLICATION PROCESS ===
STEP-BY-STEP:
1. Secure admission from recognized Korean institution; receive Certificate of Admission + Visa Issuance Confirmation
2. Complete visa application at Korean Embassy/Consulate or authorized center
3. Gather all required documents (originals + photocopies)
4. Submit application + documents
5. Pay visa fee as directed (varies by nationality)
6. Processing time: 5-7 business days standard; expedited options available
7. Upon approval: Collect passport with D-2/D-4 Visa sticker (single-entry, 90-day validity from entry)
8. Enter Korea within visa validity; apply for Alien Registration Card (ARC) within 90 days of entry

---CHUNK: Southkorea_Student_20260315_214737_chunk_11---
## Southkorea - Student Visa

Registration Card (ARC) within 90 days of entry

OBTAINING ALIEN REGISTRATION CARD (ARC):
• Must apply at local Immigration Office within 90 days of entry
• Required documents:
  - Passport with D-Visa + entry stamp
  - Certificate of Admission + Visa Issuance Confirmation (originals)
  - Proof of address in Korea (dorm confirmation, rental agreement)
  - Recent photo (3.5cm x 4.5cm)
  - Application form + fee (~KRW 30,000)
• Processing: Typically issued same day or within 2-3 weeks
• ARC serves as primary ID in Korea; must carry at all times

as primary ID in Korea; must carry at all times

PROCESSING TIMES:
• D-Visa application abroad: 5-7 business days standard; 2-3 days express
• ARC application in Korea: Same day to 2-3 weeks depending on office
• Peak seasons (Feb-Mar, Aug-Sep for academic year start): Apply 3-4 weeks in advance

D-VISA APPLICATION FEES (VARIES BY NATIONALITY):
• USA citizens: ~USD 50-90

=== VISA VALIDITY & EXTENSION ===
D-4 VISA (LANGUAGE/NON-DEGREE):
• Initial ARC validity: Typically 6 months to 1 year, matching program length
• Extension: Apply at Immigration Office at least 1 month before expiry
  - Required: Updated admission letter, proof of academic progress, financial support
  - Maximum total stay on D-4: 2 years (must change to D-2 or depart after)

-4: 2 years (must change to D-2 or depart after)

D-2 VISA (DEGREE PROGRAMS):
• Initial ARC validity: Typically 1-2 years, matching program stage
• Extension: Apply at Immigration Office at least 1 month before expiry
  - Required: Updated enrollment certificate, proof of academic progress (transcripts), financial support
  - Extension granted for remaining program duration

---CHUNK: Southkorea_Student_20260315_214737_chunk_16---

Extension granted for remaining program duration

POST-COMPLETION STAY:
• After program completion, ARC remains valid until expiry date
• Graduates may apply for:
  - Job-seeking visa (D-10): Up to 2 years to seek employment in Korea
  - Change to Work Visa (E-7) if securing employment meeting criteria
  - Departure before ARC expiry if no further status change

=== WORK RIGHTS FOR STUDENT VISA HOLDERS ===
PART-TIME WORK PERMISSION:
• D-2/D-4 Visa holders ARE PERMITTED to undertake part-time work with prior approval:
  - Must obtain permission from Immigration Office + institution
  - Maximum 20 hours/week during academic term; full-time during vacations
  - Work must not interfere with academic progress
  - Cannot work in entertainment, adult industries, or unauthorized sectors

=== OVERVIEW ===
• C-3-9 Visa: For tourism, visiting relatives/friends, short-term business meetings, medical treatment, participation in social/cultural events
• Single-entry, double-entry, or multiple-entry options available
• Validity: 3 months to 5 years (depending on nationality, reciprocity, and applicant profile)
• Duration of stay per entry: Typically 30-90 days (specified on visa sticker)
• Application via Korean Embassy/Consulate or authorized visa application center

=== VISA-EXEMPT NATIONALITIES ===
NATIONALITIES THAT CAN ENTER WITHOUT VISA FOR SHORT VISITS:
• USA, Canada, UK, most EU nations, Australia, New Zealand, Singapore, Japan, etc.: Up to 90 days visa-free
• Many Southeast Asian, Latin American nations: 30-90 days visa-free
• Full official list: https://www.visa.go.kr/openPage/main/MenuItem.do

STEP-BY-STEP:

5. Processing time: 5-7 business days standard; expedited options available (2-3 days)

VALIDITY PERIODS:

• Typically 30 days for most nationalities
• USA/Canada/EU citizens: Often granted 90 days per entry

7. Upon approval: Collect passport with E-Visa sticker (single-entry, 90-day validity from entry)
8. Enter Korea within E-Visa validity; apply for Alien Registration Card (ARC) within 90 days of entry

=== OVERVIEW ===
• Non-Immigrant O Visa: For family reunion, retirement, or other non-business purposes
• Two main subcategories:
  - O-A (Long Stay): For retirement (age 50+); apply at Thai Embassy abroad; 1-year validity
  - O (Family/Other): For spouses/children of Thai citizens or foreign residents; apply at Embassy or in Thailand
• Mandatory registration with Immigration; 90-day reporting required for long-term stays

n; 90-day reporting required for long-term stays

=== O-A RETIREMENT VISA (FOR APPLICANTS AGE 50+) ===
ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA:
□ Applicant must be aged 50 years or older at time of application
□ Hold passport valid for at least 18 months from date of application
□ Meet ONE of the following financial requirements:
  - Bank deposit in Thailand: THB 800,000 maintained for at least 2 months before application
  - Monthly income/pension: At least THB 65,000 per month (verified by Embassy/consulate)
  - Combination: Bank deposit + annual income totaling at least THB 800,000 per year
□ Have health insurance meeting Thai requirements (or purchase after arrival)
□ Provide criminal record check from home country (authenticated)
□ Pass medical examination at authorized facility (in home country or Thailand)

  - Confirming no prohibited diseases (Leprosy, Tuberculosis, Drug addiction, Elephantiasis, Syphilis 3rd stage)
  - Format: Embassy-specific or Thai Immigration form
