---CHUNK: Thailand_Student_20260315_214737_chunk_1---
## Thailand - Student Visa

| https://www.thaiembassy.org
LAST UPDATED: 2024

=== OVERVIEW ===
• Non-Immigrant ED Visa: For foreigners enrolled in recognized educational programs in Thailand
• Covers: University degrees, language courses, vocational training, Muay Thai schools, Buddhist studies, etc.
• Single-entry (90-day stay) or Multiple-entry (1-year validity) options
• Sponsored by Thai educational institution; requires acceptance letter + institution documentation
• Mandatory registration with Immigration; 90-day reporting required for long-term stays

---CHUNK: Thailand_Student_20260315_214737_chunk_2---
## Thailand - Student Visa

n; 90-day reporting required for long-term stays

=== ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA ===
APPLICANT MUST:
□ Hold passport valid for at least 6 months beyond intended study period
□ Have formal admission offer from recognized Thai educational institution
□ Demonstrate sufficient financial resources to cover tuition + living expenses in Thailand
□ Meet academic/language requirements for intended program
□ Pass health examination at authorized facility (for long-term stays)
□ Not have adverse immigration history with Thailand or other countries

---CHUNK: Thailand_Student_20260315_214737_chunk_3---
## Thailand - Student Visa

gration history with Thailand or other countries

RECOGNIZED INSTITUTIONS:
• Universities accredited by Ministry of Higher Education, Science, Research and Innovation (MHESI): https://www.mhesi.go.th
• Language schools licensed by Ministry of Education
• Vocational training centers approved by relevant authorities
• Muay Thai schools, Buddhist temples with educational programs (must be licensed)
• Verify institution recognition before applying; unlicensed institutions cannot issue valid ED visa support

---CHUNK: Thailand_Student_20260315_214737_chunk_4---
## Thailand - Student Visa

institutions cannot issue valid ED visa support

QUALIFYING PROGRAMS:
✓ Bachelor's, Master's, PhD degrees at accredited universities
✓ Thai language programs (semester/year-long) at university language centers or licensed schools
✓ Vocational training programs (cooking, massage, hospitality, etc.) at licensed institutions
✓ Muay Thai training programs at licensed camps/schools
✓ Buddhist studies/meditation programs at licensed temples
✓ Exchange programs, visiting scholar programs with formal institutional agreement

lar programs with formal institutional agreement

NON-QUALIFYING PROGRAMS:
✗ Informal/unlicensed language schools or training centers
✗ Online/distance learning programs without physical presence in Thailand
✗ Short-term tourism-style "study tours" without formal academic enrollment

=== DOCUMENT REQUIREMENTS ===

---CHUNK: Thailand_Student_20260315_214737_chunk_6---
## Thailand - Student Visa

ademic enrollment

=== DOCUMENT REQUIREMENTS ===

#### NON-IMMIGRANT ED VISA APPLICATION (ABROAD)
MANDATORY DOCUMENTS:
□ Completed visa application form (https://www.thaievisa.go.th or Embassy form)
□ Recent passport-sized photograph (4x6 cm, white background)
□ Original passport (valid 6+ months beyond intended study)
□ Photocopy of passport biodata page
□ Acceptance Letter from Thai institution (original + copy):
  - On official letterhead, signed, with institution seal
  - Details: program name, duration, start/end dates, tuition fees
□ Institution Documentation:
  - Copy of institution's license/registration from Ministry of Education/MHESI
  - Letter confirming institution's authorization to enroll foreign students
□ Proof of financial means:
  - Bank statements (last 3-6 months) showing sufficient funds (~THB 20,000-50,000 recommended for 1 year)
  - Scholarship award letter, OR
  - Sponsorship letter + sponsor's financial documents + proof of relationship
□ Educational qualifications: Highest degree certificate + transcript (authenticated if issued outside Thailand)
□ For language programs: Proof of prior language study or placement test results (if required)

ge study or placement test results (if required)

ADDITIONAL DOCUMENTS (MAY BE REQUESTED):
□ Study plan/personal statement explaining educational goals
□ Letters of recommendation from previous professors/employers
□ Health Examination Certificate (for long-term stays):
  - Conducted at authorized facility; report valid for 3 months
  - Tests: Chest X-ray (TB screening), blood tests, physical exam
□ Criminal Record Check (for certain nationalities/programs)
□ For minors (<18): Parental consent letter, guardian details in Thailand

---CHUNK: Thailand_Student_20260315_214737_chunk_8---
## Thailand - Student Visa

tal consent letter, guardian details in Thailand

=== APPLICATION PROCESS ===
STEP-BY-STEP:
1. Secure admission from recognized Thai institution; receive Acceptance Letter + institution documentation
2. Complete visa application at Thai Embassy/Consulate or authorized center
3. Gather all required documents (originals + photocopies)
4. Submit application + documents
5. Pay visa fee as directed:
   - Single-Entry ED Visa: ~USD 80 (~THB 2,800)
   - Multiple-Entry ED Visa (1-year): ~USD 200 (~THB 7,000)
6. Processing time: 3-5 business days standard; expedited options available
7. Upon approval: Collect passport with ED Visa sticker (single-entry, 90-day validity from entry)
8. Enter Thailand within ED Visa validity; report address to Immigration within 24 hours of arrival
9. For programs >90 days: Apply for visa extension at Immigration Office before initial 90 days expire

---CHUNK: Thailand_Student_20260315_214737_chunk_9---
## Thailand - Student Visa

Immigration Office before initial 90 days expire

VISA EXTENSION PROCESS (IN THAILAND):
• Apply at local Immigration Office at least 30 days before initial 90-day stay expires
• Required documents:
  - Passport with ED Visa + entry stamp
  - Acceptance Letter + institution documentation (originals + copies)
  - Proof of tuition payment for extension period
  - Proof of address in Thailand (rental agreement, dorm confirmation)
  - Recent photo (4x6 cm)
  - TM.7 extension form + fee (~THB 1,900 per 90-day extension)
• Processing: Typically 7-15 business days; applicant may stay in Thailand during processing with acknowledgment receipt
• Extensions granted in 90-day increments up to program duration

• ED Visa application abroad: 3-5 business days standard; 1-2 days express

=== WORK RIGHTS FOR ED VISA HOLDERS ===
PART-TIME WORK PERMISSION:
• ED Visa holders ARE PERMITTED to undertake part-time work with prior approval:
  - Must obtain permission from Immigration Office + educational institution
  - Maximum 20 hours/week during academic term; full-time during vacations
  - Work must not interfere with academic progress
  - Cannot work in prohibited occupations (see Work Visa file)

Thailand offers three main entry options for tourists:

## Thailand - Tourist Visa

nd offers three main entry options for tourists:

1. VISA EXEMPTION: For nationals of 64+ countries; enter without visa for 30 days (air) or 15 days (land)
2. VISA ON ARRIVAL (VOA): For nationals of 19 countries; obtain 15-day visa at Thai airport/land border
3. TOURIST VISA (TR): Single-entry (60 days) or Multiple-entry (6 months validity); apply at Thai Embassy/Consulate

=== OVERSTAY PENALTIES ===
CONSEQUENCES OF OVERSTAYING:
• Fine: THB 500 per day of overstay (max THB 20,000)
• Detention/deportation for overstays >90 days
• Entry ban: 1 year (overstay <90 days), 3 years (90 days-1 year), 5 years (1-3 years), 10 years (3+ years), permanent (5+ years)
• Future Thai visa applications will face additional scrutiny or refusal

## Thailand - Work Visa

| https://www.thaiembassy.org
LAST UPDATED: 2024

=== OVERVIEW ===
• Non-Immigrant B Visa: For foreigners taking up employment or business activities in Thailand
• Single-entry (90-day stay) or Multiple-entry (1-year validity) options
• MUST obtain Work Permit from Department of Employment (DOE) within 90 days of entry
• Sponsored by Thai employer; employer must meet capital/foreign employee ratio requirements
• Mandatory registration with Immigration; 90-day reporting required for long-term stays

---CHUNK: Thailand_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_2---
## Thailand - Work Visa

n; 90-day reporting required for long-term stays

=== ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA ===
APPLICANT MUST:
□ Have valid job offer/employment contract from Thai company registered to hire foreigners
□ Possess qualifications meeting job requirements (degree, experience, certifications)
□ Receive minimum salary meeting Immigration/DOE guidelines (varies by nationality/industry)
□ Pass health examination at authorized facility (for Work Permit application)
□ Have no criminal record in home country or Thailand
□ Not be on prohibited occupation list for foreigners (see below)

---CHUNK: Thailand_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_3---

bited occupation list for foreigners (see below)

PROHIBITED OCCUPATIONS FOR FOREIGNERS:
✗ Manual labor, agriculture, animal husbandry, forestry, fishery
✗ Wood carving, driving vehicles/machinery (except international pilots)
✗ Auctioneering, hairdressing, weaving, handicrafts
✗ Tourist guiding, street vending, certain retail roles
• Full list: Ministerial Regulation on Prohibited Occupations for Aliens B.E. 2522

✓ Specialists with expertise not readily available in Thai labor market

=== APPLICATION PROCESS ===
STEP-BY-STEP:
1. Thai employer prepares Work Permit support documents + applies for Ministry of Labour approval (if required)
2. Applicant applies for Non-Immigrant B Visa at Thai Embassy/Consulate abroad
3. Submit visa application + documents; pay fee (~USD 80-200 depending on entry type)
4. Processing: 3-5 business days standard; expedited options available
5. Upon approval: Collect passport with B Visa sticker (single-entry, 90-day validity from entry)
6. Enter Thailand within B Visa validity
7. Employer submits Work Permit application to Department of Employment within 90 days of entry
8. Upon Work Permit approval: Employee receives Work Permit book/card
9. Employee must report address to Immigration within 24 hours of arrival; 90-day reporting thereafter

---CHUNK: Thailand_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_10---
## Thailand - Work Visa

24 hours of arrival; 90-day reporting thereafter

PROCESSING TIMES:
• B Visa application abroad: 3-5 business days standard; 1-2 days express
• Work Permit application in Thailand: 7-15 business days standard; expedited options available
• Ministry of Labour approval (if required): 2-4 weeks

=== FEES (APPROXIMATE, USD/THB) ===
NON-IMMIGRANT B VISA FEES (VARIES BY NATIONALITY/EMBASSY):
• Single-Entry: ~USD 80 (~THB 2,800)
• Multiple-Entry (1-year): ~USD 200 (~THB 7,000)

=== TAX & COMPLIANCE OBLIGATIONS ===
INCOME TAX:
• Foreign employees are tax residents if stay in Thailand exceeds 180 days in a calendar year
• Must obtain Tax ID from Revenue Department
• Employer typically withholds Personal Income Tax (PIT); file annual tax return (March each year)
• Tax rates: Progressive 5-35% based on income

---CHUNK: Thailand_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_18---

)
• Tax rates: Progressive 5-35% based on income

SOCIAL SECURITY:
• Foreign employees generally required to contribute to Social Security Fund (if employer has 1+ Thai employees)
• Contribution: 5% of salary (capped at THB 750/month) shared between employer/employee
• Benefits: Healthcare, maternity, disability, death, pension

• Foreign employees have same rights as Thai employees under most labor statutes
• Disputes resolved via local labor courts or mediation

ae | https://www.mohap.gov.ae

=== OVERVIEW ===
• Expatriate residents with valid UAE residence permit can sponsor family members for residence visas
• Sponsor must meet minimum salary requirement: AED 4,000/month OR AED 3,000/month + valid accommodation
• Sponsored family members receive residence visas linked to sponsor's visa validity (except parents: yearly visas)
• Medical fitness test mandatory for sponsored members aged 18+ at approved UAE health centers
• Profession type no longer a barrier to family sponsorship eligibility

=== APPLICATION PROCESS ===
CHANNELS:

#### DIGITAL (ICP SMART SERVICES / GDRFA DUBAI)
STEPS:
1. Login to https://smartservices.icp.gov.ae or https://www.gdrfad.gov.ae
2. Select "Sponsor Family" service
3. Fill application form with sponsor and dependent details
4. Upload required documents (passport copies, photos, marriage/birth certificates, salary proof, accommodation proof)
5. Pay fees online via credit/debit card
6. Receive application reference number for tracking
7. Await approval notification (2-4 weeks standard)
8. Dependent enters UAE on entry permit; sponsor has 60 days to complete residence visa issuance
9. Complete medical exam (if dependent 18+), biometrics, Emirates ID registration
10. Collect residence visa + Emirates ID

#### IN-PERSON (TYPING CENTERS / AMER CENTERS)
STEPS:

2. Submit completed application form + all required documents
3. Staff enters application into system; verifies documents on-spot
4. Pay fees via cash, card, or local payment methods
5. Receive receipt with reference number
6. Track application status online using reference number
7. Upon approval: Dependent enters UAE; complete medical exam, biometrics, ID registration within 60 days

=== CANCELLATION & GRACE PERIOD ===
WHEN SPONSOR'S VISA IS CANCELLED:
• Dependents' visas automatically cancelled simultaneously
• 6-month grace period from cancellation date for dependents to:
  - Obtain new sponsorship (new employer, family member, or investor visa)
  - Change status to tourist visa and depart UAE
  - Apply for Golden Visa or other long-term residence if eligible

• Potential entry ban (6 months to permanent) for excessive overstay
• Future UAE visa applications face additional scrutiny

## Uae - Student Visa

VISA TYPE: UAE Golden Visa (Long-Term Residence Visa - 5 or 10 Years)
COUNTRY: United Arab Emirates
SOURCE: https://www.icp.gov.ae | https://www.gdrfad.gov.ae | https://www.tamm.abudhabi
LAST UPDATED: 2024

---CHUNK: Uae_Student_20260315_214737_chunk_1---
## Uae - Student Visa

e | https://www.tamm.abudhabi
LAST UPDATED: 2024

=== OVERVIEW & KEY BENEFITS ===
• Long-term renewable residence visa: 5 years (real estate investors, entrepreneurs, students) or 10 years (public investors, outstanding talents, humanitarian pioneers)
• No sponsor required within UAE
• Multiple-entry entry visa (6 months validity) to complete residence issuance
• Privilege to stay outside UAE for more than 6 months without visa cancellation
• Sponsor family members: spouses, children (any age), parents (under conditions)
• Sponsor unlimited domestic helpers
• Family members retain residence validity if primary holder passes away
• Pathway to long-term stability in UAE for eligible foreign talents

---CHUNK: Uae_Student_20260315_214737_chunk_2---
## Uae - Student Visa

rm stability in UAE for eligible foreign talents

=== ELIGIBILITY CATEGORIES & REQUIREMENTS ===

s

=== ELIGIBILITY CATEGORIES & REQUIREMENTS ===

#### 1. INVESTORS IN PUBLIC INVESTMENTS (10-YEAR VISA)
ELIGIBILITY:
□ Invest at least AED 2 million in an accredited UAE investment fund
  • Submit letter from fund confirming deposit amount
□ OR Hold valid commercial/industrial license with MoA showing capital ≥ AED 2 million
□ OR Pay annual government taxes ≥ AED 250,000 (verified by Federal Tax Authority letter)
□ Own invested capital completely (not borrowed/loaned)
□ Provide proof of medical insurance for self and family (if sponsoring)

---CHUNK: Uae_Student_20260315_214737_chunk_4---

al insurance for self and family (if sponsoring)

#### 2. REAL ESTATE INVESTORS (5-YEAR VISA, RENEWABLE)
ELIGIBILITY:
□ Own one or more properties valued at ≥ AED 2 million (verified by emirate Land Department letter)
□ Property purchase can be financed via loan from specific local banks approved by competent local entity
□ Property must be completed (off-plan properties may have additional conditions)
□ Maintain ownership throughout visa validity for renewal eligibility

□ Approval from emirate authorities confirming project is technical/future-oriented
□ Approval from accredited UAE business incubator for proposed activity
□ Business must be registered and operational in UAE

=== APPLICATION PROCESS ===
STEP-BY-STEP:
1. Determine eligibility category and gather required documents
2. Submit pre-approval application via:
   • ICP Smart Services: https://smartservices.icp.gov.ae
   • GDRFA Dubai: https://www.gdrfad.gov.ae
   • TAMM Abu Dhabi: https://www.tamm.abudhabi
   • Authorized typing centers or Amer centers
3. Receive initial approval notification (if eligible)
4. Complete medical examination at MOHAP-approved health center
5. Submit biometrics (fingerprints, photo) at authorized ICP center
6. Pay visa issuance fees and Emirates ID fees
7. Receive Golden Visa residence permit + Emirates ID card

=== VISA CANCELLATION CONDITIONS ===
GOLDEN VISA MAY BE CANCELLED IF:
✗ Holder obtains residence in another country and abandons UAE residency
✗ Holder is convicted of serious crime or poses security threat to UAE
✗ Fraudulent documents or misrepresentation discovered during validity period
✗ Investor category: Investment withdrawn or falls below AED 2 million threshold
✗ Talent category: No longer practicing in approved field or losing ministry endorsements
✗ Student category: Discontinued studies or failed to maintain required academic standards
✗ Violation of UAE laws or immigration regulations

=== TRANSITION TO CITIZENSHIP ===
CURRENT POLICY:
• Golden Visa is a long-term residence permit, NOT a direct pathway to UAE citizenship
• UAE citizenship is granted through separate, highly selective process (Royal Decree)
• Long-term residency via Golden Visa may strengthen future citizenship consideration but is not guaranteed

---CHUNK: Uae_Student_20260315_214737_chunk_32---
## Uae - Student Visa

citizenship consideration but is not guaranteed

ALTERNATIVE PATHWAYS TO CITIZENSHIP:
• Naturalization: Typically requires 30 years continuous residence (reduced for certain categories like scientists, artists)
• Marriage to UAE national: Possible pathway with specific conditions and approval
• Exceptional contribution: Scientists, artists, investors may be considered for citizenship via special Royal Decree
• Note: Citizenship decisions are at discretion of UAE leadership; no automatic entitlement

SOURCE: https://www.gdrfad.gov.ae | https://www.icp.gov.ae
LAST UPDATED: 2024

=== OVERVIEW ===
• Multi-entry tourist visa valid for 5 years from date of issue
• No guarantor or host required within UAE
• For travelers not eligible for visa-on-arrival or visa-free entry
• Purpose: Tourism, visiting family/friends, short business visits (NO employment)

---CHUNK: Uae_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_1---
## Uae - Tourist Visa

y/friends, short business visits (NO employment)

=== ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA ===
APPLICANT MUST:
□ Hold passport or travel document valid for at least 6 months from intended entry date
□ Passport must allow entry into UAE and return to country of residence/issuance
□ Provide proof of bank balance: USD 4,000 (or equivalent) maintained over 6 months prior to application
□ Hold valid health insurance covering UAE stay
□ Possess round-trip ticket or onward travel ticket
□ Not be subject to UAE entry ban or immigration violation
□ Intend stay of max 90 days per entry (extendable once), max 180 days total per calendar year

---CHUNK: Uae_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_2---
## Uae - Tourist Visa

able once), max 180 days total per calendar year

=== DOCUMENT REQUIREMENTS ===
MANDATORY DOCUMENTS:
□ Personal photograph:
  • Recent color photo (within 6 months)
  • Size: 4.3 x 5.5 cm (passport-sized)
  • White/light blue background, neutral expression, face fully visible
  • Digital format: JPG/PNG, 300 DPI minimum for online applications

  • Must allow return to country of residence/issuance

□ Bank statement:
  • Official statement from recognized bank covering last 6 months
  • Must show consistent balance of at least USD 4,000 (or equivalent)
  • Stamped/signed by bank; in English or Arabic (or certified translation)

  • Policy document showing applicant name, coverage amount, validity dates
  • Minimum recommended coverage: ~AED 150,000 (~USD 40,000)
  • Must cover emergency medical treatment, hospitalization, repatriation
  • Valid for entire duration of intended UAE stay

□ Round-trip ticket:
  • Confirmed flight reservation showing entry and exit from UAE
  • Can be provisional booking; final ticket not required at application stage

=== FEES (APPROXIMATE) ===
APPLICATION FEE BREAKDOWN:
• Application Fee: AED 100
• Issuance Fee: AED 500
• Guarantee Amount: AED 3,000 (refundable upon compliance)
• Warranty Service Fee: AED 21
• Guarantee Collection/Return Fee: AED 20
• Knowledge Dirham: AED 10
• Innovation Dirham: AED 10
• Service Fee: AED 52.50
• **Estimated Total: AED 3,713.50** (~USD 1,010)

IMPORTANT NOTES:
• Total amount may vary based on applicant circumstances, emirate, or service channel
• Guarantee amount (AED 3,000) is refundable if visa conditions are met
• Payment methods: Credit/debit card (online), cash/card (in-person centers)
• Fees are non-refundable if application is rejected

=== APPLICATION CHANNELS ===

#### DIGITAL CHANNELS (UAE PASS / ICP SMART SERVICES)
STEPS:
1. Log in to smart services system via UAE Pass or username/password
2. Search for "5-Year Multi-Entry Tourist Visa" service
3. Fill in application form with personal, passport, and travel details
4. Upload required documents (photo, passport copy, bank statement, insurance, ticket)
5. Pay service fees online via credit/debit card
6. Receive application reference number for tracking
7. Await approval notification via email/SMS (2-5 working days standard)
8. Download e-visa upon approval; print or save digitally for travel

#### CUSTOMER HAPPINESS CENTERS (GDRFA)

5. Pay fees via cash, card, or local payment methods
6. Receive application receipt with reference number
7. Await approval notification (2-5 working days)
8. Collect visa sticker or receive e-visa notification

=== STAY CONDITIONS & LIMITS ===
PER-ENTRY STAY:
• Maximum 90 consecutive days per entry into UAE
• Clock resets upon exit and re-entry

EXTENSION OPTION:
• Can apply to extend 90-day stay once for additional 90 days
• Must apply BEFORE current stay period expires
• Extension fee: ~AED 600-800 (varies by emirate)
• Processing: ~2-5 working days
• Total stay cannot exceed 180 days within any calendar year

ANNUAL LIMIT:
• Maximum 180 days total stay in UAE per calendar year across all entries
• Days counted from entry stamp to exit stamp (include partial days)
• Exceeding limit may result in visa cancellation and future application issues

=== ENTRY TO UAE ===
AT PORT OF ENTRY:
• Present: Passport with visa (printed or digital), return/onward ticket, health insurance proof if requested
• Immigration officer may ask: Purpose of visit, accommodation details, funds proof, travel itinerary
• Biometrics: Fingerprints and photo may be collected (standard procedure)

=== COMPLIANCE & PENALTIES ===
OVERSTAY FINES:
• First day of overstay: AED 125
• Each subsequent day: AED 25
• Additional service fees may apply for fine payment

---CHUNK: Uae_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_23---
## Uae - Tourist Visa

ditional service fees may apply for fine payment

CONSEQUENCES OF NON-COMPLIANCE:
• Must pay all fines before departure or future visa applications
• Excessive overstay may result in:
  - Entry ban (6 months to permanent)
  - Deportation at applicant's expense
  - Future visa applications refused
  - Difficulty obtaining visas for other countries

GRACE PERIOD:
• Typically 10 days after visa expiry to leave UAE or apply for extension
• NOT guaranteed; always confirm current policy with GDRFA/ICP
• Overstay fines may still accrue during grace period in some cases

=== REJECTION & REAPPLICATION ===
COMMON REFUSAL GROUNDS:
✗ Insufficient or unclear bank balance proof
✗ Passport validity <6 months or damaged passport
✗ Previous UAE immigration violations (overstay, deportation, ban)
✗ Security concerns or adverse background checks
✗ Incomplete/unclear application information or document quality issues
✗ Health insurance not meeting requirements

sues

REAPPLICATION GUIDELINES:
• Address specific refusal reason with stronger, clearer documentation
• Wait at least 30 days before reapplying unless circumstances changed significantly
• For security-related refusals: May require special clearance from UAE authorities
• Consider applying through authorized travel agent for guidance on complex cases
• Ensure all documents are translated to English/Arabic by certified translator if needed

=== VISA-EXEMPT & VISA-ON-ARRIVAL CONTEXT ===
WHO DOES NOT NEED THIS VISA:
• GCC citizens (Bahrain, Kuwait, Oman, Qatar, Saudi Arabia): No visa required with national ID
• ~50 nationalities eligible for 30-day visa-on-arrival (extendable once): USA, UK, Canada, Australia, EU, Japan, South Korea, Singapore, etc.
• Select nationalities eligible for 90-day visa-on-arrival (non-extendable): Mexico, Seychelles, etc.

---CHUNK: Uae_Tourist_20260315_214737_chunk_32---
## Uae - Tourist Visa

rival (non-extendable): Mexico, Seychelles, etc.

WHY CHOOSE 5-YEAR MULTI-ENTRY VISA:
• Frequent travelers to UAE wanting convenience of pre-approved visa
• Nationalities not eligible for visa-on-arrival
• Travelers wanting longer validity than standard 30/90-day tourist visas
• Business visitors making multiple short trips (without employment)

## Uae - Work Visa

VISA TYPE: UAE Green Visa for Work (5-Year Self-Sponsored Residence Visa)
COUNTRY: United Arab Emirates
SOURCE: https://www.icp.gov.ae | https://www.mohre.gov.ae | https://www.gdrfad.gov.ae

---CHUNK: Uae_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_1---
## Uae - Work Visa

e | https://www.gdrfad.gov.ae
LAST UPDATED: 2024

=== OVERVIEW ===
• 5-year renewable residence visa that allows holder to sponsor themselves
• No requirement for UAE national or employer sponsorship
• Eligible categories: Freelancers/self-employed individuals, skilled employees
• Provides greater flexibility and stability compared to standard employer-sponsored visas
• Holders can sponsor family members (subject to standard family sponsorship requirements)

---CHUNK: Uae_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_2---

=== ELIGIBILITY CATEGORIES & REQUIREMENTS ===

#### 1. FREELANCERS AND SELF-EMPLOYED INDIVIDUALS
ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA:
□ Hold valid freelance/self-employment permit from Ministry of Human Resources and Emiratisation (MOHRE)
□ Hold bachelor's degree OR specialized diploma relevant to freelance activity
□ Provide ONE of the following financial proofs:
   • Evidence of annual income from self-employment ≥ AED 360,000 for each of previous two years, OR
   • Proof of financial solvency throughout intended stay in UAE

---CHUNK: Uae_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_4---
## Uae - Work Visa

nancial solvency throughout intended stay in UAE

FREELANCE PERMIT REQUIREMENTS:
• Apply via MOHRE Freelance Portal: https://www.mohre.gov.ae/freelance
• Eligible activities: Media, marketing, consulting, education, technology, design, arts, etc.
• Permit validity: 1-3 years (renewable)
• Fee: ~AED 7,500-15,000 depending on activity and emirate

## Uae - Work Visa

D 7,500-15,000 depending on activity and emirate

FINANCIAL PROOF OPTIONS:
INCOME-BASED (AED 360,000/YEAR):
• Bank statements showing consistent freelance income deposits
• Client contracts/invoices demonstrating project revenue
• Tax returns from UAE or home country (converted to AED)
• Average calculation: AED 30,000/month over 24 months

#### 2. SKILLED EMPLOYEES
ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA:
□ Hold valid employment contract with UAE-based employer
□ Be classified in first, second, or third occupational level per MOHRE classification
□ Hold minimum bachelor's degree or equivalent (attested)
□ Receive monthly salary of not less than AED 15,000 (gross, fixed components only)

SALARY VERIFICATION RULES:
• AED 15,000 minimum refers to GROSS monthly salary (basic + fixed allowances)

• EXCLUDED: Bonuses, commissions, overtime pay, variable incentives
• Verified via: Employment contract, Wage Protection System (WPS) records, bank statements

=== APPLICATION PROCESS ===
STEP-BY-STEP GUIDE:
1. Determine eligibility category and gather required documents
2. Submit application via:
   • ICP Smart Services: https://smartservices.icp.gov.ae
   • GDRFA Dubai: https://www.gdrfad.gov.ae
   • Authorized typing centers or Amer centers
3. Pay application fees online or at service center
4. Complete medical examination at MOHAP-approved health center
5. Submit biometrics (fingerprints, photo) at ICP center
6. Receive initial approval notification
7. Pay issuance fees and collect Green Visa residence permit + Emirates ID

=== MEDICAL EXAMINATION REQUIREMENTS ===
MANDATORY FOR ALL GREEN VISA APPLICANTS:
• Conducted at MOHAP-approved health centers in UAE
• Tests: Chest X-ray (TB screening), blood tests (HIV, Hepatitis B/C, Syphilis), general physical exam
• Results typically available within 24-48 hours
• Medical fitness certificate valid for 3 months for visa issuance

---CHUNK: Uae_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_20---

certificate valid for 3 months for visa issuance

EXEMPTIONS:
• Applicants under 18 may have reduced testing requirements
• Dormant/inactive pulmonary tuberculosis: May receive one-year conditional certificate subject to treatment

APPROVED HEALTH CENTERS:
• Abu Dhabi: Disease Prevention & Screening Center, SEHA facilities
• Dubai: Dubai Health Authority (DHA) approved centers
• Other Emirates: Emirates Health Services facilities
• Full list: https://www.mohap.gov.ae

=== FAMILY SPONSORSHIP RIGHTS ===
ELIGIBILITY TO SPONSOR FAMILY:
• Green Visa holders CAN sponsor family members (spouse, children, parents)
• Standard family sponsorship requirements apply:
  - Minimum salary: AED 4,000/month OR AED 3,000 + valid accommodation
  - Valid accommodation meeting emirate occupancy standards
  - Medical insurance for sponsored parents (if applicable)

ADVANTAGES OVER STANDARD VISA:
• Green Visa validity (5 years) provides longer stability for sponsored dependents
• No employer dependency: Family visas not affected if Green Visa holder changes jobs or becomes unemployed (as long as Green Visa remains valid)

APPLICATION PROCESS FOR DEPENDENTS:
• Submit separate family sponsorship application via ICP/GDRFA portal
• Required: Green Visa copy, salary proof, accommodation proof, relationship documents (attested marriage/birth certificates)
• Processing: 2-4 weeks standard
• Fees: ~AED 1,500-2,500 per dependent (spouse/child); ~AED 2,000-3,500 per parent (includes deposit + insurance)

=== RENEWAL PROCESS (EVERY 5 YEARS) ===
ELIGIBILITY FOR RENEWAL:
• Freelancers: Must maintain valid MOHRE freelance permit AND continue to meet income/solvency requirements
• Skilled employees: Must maintain qualifying employment OR secure new qualifying job within 6 months of previous employment ending
• No criminal record or immigration violations during visa validity
• Valid passport (6+ months remaining at renewal application)

ort (6+ months remaining at renewal application)

RENEWAL STEPS:
1. Submit renewal application via ICP/GDRFA portal 30-90 days before expiry

   • Freelancers: Renewed freelance permit, updated income/financial proof
   • Skilled employees: New/continued employment contract, updated salary proof, MOHRE occupational confirmation

=== VISA CANCELLATION CONDITIONS ===
GREEN VISA MAY BE CANCELLED IF:
✗ Freelancer: Loses MOHRE freelance permit OR income falls below threshold for 2 consecutive years
✗ Skilled employee: Employment contract terminated AND no new qualifying job secured within 6-month grace period
✗ Holder convicted of serious crime or poses security threat to UAE
✗ Fraudulent documents or misrepresentation discovered during validity period
✗ Holder abandons UAE residency (stays outside UAE >6 months continuously without valid reason)
✗ Violation of UAE laws or immigration regulations

Violation of UAE laws or immigration regulations

• If employment ends: 6-month grace period to secure new qualifying job
• During grace period: Green Visa remains valid; holder can stay in UAE, sponsor family, seek new employment
• If no new job secured within 6 months: Visa may be cancelled; dependent visas affected simultaneously

You need a family visa to live with a family member in the UK for more than 6 months.
Eligible relationships: spouse, partner, fiancé(e), child, parent, relative providing long-term care.

• 20 points: Salary criteria (meet general threshold OR going rate for occupation OR new entrant rate)

## Usa - Work Visa

VISA TYPE: H-1B Specialty Occupation (Work Visa)
COUNTRY: USA

---CHUNK: Usa_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_1---
## Usa - Work Visa

1B Specialty Occupation (Work Visa)
COUNTRY: USA

ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA - EMPLOYER (PETITIONER):
- Must offer a job that qualifies as a "specialty occupation" (requires theoretical/practical application of highly specialized knowledge).
- Must demonstrate a valid employer-employee relationship with the beneficiary.
- Must file a Labor Condition Application (LCA) with the Department of Labor and certify compliance with wage requirements.
- Must agree to pay the higher of the actual wage or the prevailing wage for the occupation in the area of employment.
- Must pay required filing fees (including ACWIA fee, Fraud Prevention fee if applicable).

---CHUNK: Usa_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_2---
## Usa - Work Visa

ACWIA fee, Fraud Prevention fee if applicable).

ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA - APPLICANT (BENEFICIARY):
- Must possess at least a bachelor's degree or its equivalent in a field directly related to the specialty occupation.
- If degree is from outside the US, it must be evaluated as equivalent to a US degree.
- If lacking a degree, must demonstrate equivalent expertise through progressive work experience (typically 3 years of experience = 1 year of college).
- Must be coming to the US to work in the specialty occupation for which they are qualified.
- Must maintain valid immigration status if already in the US.

---CHUNK: Usa_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_3---
## Usa - Work Visa

n valid immigration status if already in the US.

ADDITIONAL REQUIREMENTS:
- Position must require a degree as a minimum entry requirement (not preferred, but required).
- The nature of the duties must be so specialized and complex that the knowledge required to perform them is usually associated with a bachelor's degree or higher.
- Most H-1B petitions are subject to an annual cap (65,000 regular + 20,000 for US advanced degree holders), unless exempt (e.g., higher education, nonprofit research).

---CHUNK: Usa_Work_20260315_214737_chunk_4---
## Usa - Work Visa

pt (e.g., higher education, nonprofit research).

DOCUMENTS TYPICALLY REQUIRED:
- Copy of beneficiary's degree(s) and transcripts
- Credential evaluation for foreign degrees
- Detailed job description showing specialty occupation requirements
- Approved Labor Condition Application (LCA)
